# Brave Little Days — Season 1 Drafts (Unbuilt Episodes)

> Yapılmayan Sezon 1 bölümleri için **hafif taslaklar** — logline, mekan, kadro, tekrarlanan cümle,
> 8 shot / 6 adımlı omurga (Problem → Feeling → Support → Action → Relief → Lesson) ve uyarılar.
> Bunlar **tam paket değildir**; onaylandıktan sonra `.../04_EPISODE_PACKAGES/` altında tam pakete
> dönüştürülür. Plan/numaralandırma: `SEASON_01_PLAN.md`. Format: `00-CORE/32_BRAVE_LITTLE_DAYS_LIFE_SKILLS_FORMAT.md`.
>
> Durum: **BLD-EP08–BLD-EP20 için 13 adet Scene Definition Starter hazır.** Her starter'da
> 8-shot omurga vardır; her bölüm için Shot 01 detay tanımı eklenmiştir. Bunlar hâlâ **tam
> episode package değildir**; onaylandıktan sonra `.../04_EPISODE_PACKAGES/` altında tam pakete
> dönüştürülür. ⭐ = kullanıcı must-have · 🆕 = yeni canon kararı gerekir.
>
> **Onay bekleyen starter'lar:** BLD-EP14 (light crowd + safe helper), BLD-EP15 (Pompom Crossing
> soft practice path), BLD-EP17 (Learning Room production/drop-off kullanımı), BLD-EP20
> (soft clean-up bin/basket prop'u).

---

## BLD-EP08 — "Share and Play" (viewing #8)

- **Tema:** Paylaşmayı öğrenmek · **Mekan:** Central Square / Benny's Playground · **Kadro:** Kiko, Amara
- **Repeated phrase:** "Sharing is more fun."
- **Spine:** (1) Kiko'nun bir oyuncağı var, Amara da oynamak ister. (2) Kiko sıkıca tutar, "It's mine."
  (3) Amara üzülür; Kiko duraksar. (4) Kiko oyuncağı paylaşır / sırayla verir. (5) Birlikte oynamak daha
  eğlenceli olur. (6) "Sharing is more fun." (7) İkisi de güler. (8) Sıcak kapanış.
- **Not:** Viewing #7 "taking turns" çekirdek S01E10 ile çakıştığı için, o başlık yerine bu "paylaşma"
  bölümü öneriliyor (izin isteme beat'i buraya katılabilir). Yeni canon yok.

### Scene Definition Starter (başlandı)

- **Kapsam kararı:** Tek ana set olarak **Benny's Playground — Ball Pit Area** önerilir.
  Central Square sadece yakınlık/navigasyon bağlamıdır; story shot'larında yeni mekan geçişi
  açılmadan playground içinde kalmak continuity açısından daha güvenlidir.
- **Prop:** Canon `BP-BALLPIT-01` içinden tek bir yumuşak mor/top pastel top. Yeni oyuncak canon'u yok.
- **Çakışma önleme:** Bu bölüm "sırayla oynama" değil, **aynı şeyi birlikte paylaşma** üzerine kuruludur.
  Top el değiştirme oyunu minimumda tutulur; asıl çözüm topu birlikte yuvarlamak/oyuna birlikte dahil etmektir.

| Shot | Spine | Scene amacı | Kısa tanım |
|---:|---|---|---|
| 01 | Problem | Oyuncağı kur | Kiko, Ball Pit Area'da yumuşak mor bir top bulur; Amara yakından gülümseyerek bakar. |
| 02 | Feeling | Sahiplenme hissi | Kiko topu göğsüne sarar: "It's mine." Amara'nın gülümsemesi hafifçe düşer. |
| 03 | Support | İzin isteme + fark etme | Amara yumuşakça sorar: "Can I play too?" Kiko durur ve Amara'nın yüzünü fark eder. |
| 04 | Action | Paylaşmaya başlama | Kiko topu ikisinin arasına indirir: "You can play too." |
| 05 | Action | Birlikte oyun | İkisi topu yavaşça birbirlerine değil, birlikte çizdikleri küçük bir daire yolunda yuvarlar. |
| 06 | Relief | Paylaşmanın keyfi | Top oyunu iki kişiyle daha eğlenceli olur; ikisi de güler. "Sharing is more fun." |
| 07 | Relief | Kiko'nun içselleştirmesi | Kiko topu Amara'ya doğru iter, sonra beraber geri getirir; Kiko rahat ve gururludur. |
| 08 | Lesson | Sıcak kapanış | Kiko ve Amara topu aralarında tutup küçük dalga verir: "Sharing is more fun." |

#### BLD-EP08 — Shot 08 — Warm Closing (Lesson)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP08 — Share and Play |
| Shot | 08 / 08 |
| Duration | 12 seconds |
| Location | Benny's Playground — Ball Pit Area |
| Characters | Kiko, Amara |
| Time of Day | Warm Morning |
| Spine step | LESSON |

## Purpose

The warm closing shot: Kiko and Amara hold the ball together and give a small wave to the
camera. The repeated phrase "Sharing is more fun" is delivered one final time, sealing the
lesson with a friendly goodbye.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Both characters hold the purple ball together between them, kneeling on
the grass. They look at the camera with warm, relaxed smiles.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 07. The ball has been rolling back and forth between them. Now
they hold it together — a shared object in shared hands. Background remains locked.

## Environment Anchors

- Same Benny's Playground Ball Pit Area; blue slide remains as landmark.
- `BP-BALLPIT-01` visible behind Kiko.
- The soft purple ball is held jointly between Kiko and Amara.
- Both characters are kneeling, facing the camera.
- No new props, no new characters, no background movement.

## Background Object Lock

Identical to Shots 01–07. Background locked from first frame. Only Kiko and Amara move.
The ball pit, blue slide, grass, and rounded equipment remain stable.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Benny's Playground Ball Pit Area, warm morning. Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown pigtails) and
Amara (yellow shirt, purple short overalls, yellow bow headband, two dark brown puff buns) kneel
on the soft grass, holding the soft purple playground ball together between them. Both face the
camera with warm, relaxed smiles. They say: "Sharing is more fun." Then they give a small gentle
wave. Soft pastel colours, warm light, rounded safe playground shapes, no other characters, {style}
{camera} {lighting}

The Benny's Playground background is locked from the first frame; keep the blue slide, ball pit,
soft grass and rounded equipment stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

Medium shot at child eye level, both characters centered in frame. Camera holds steady for the
final moment. A very gentle, almost imperceptible pull-back to show the full warm scene. The
shot fades to soft warmth at the end.

## Dialogue

```text
Kiko & Amara: Sharing is more fun!
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-3 sec | Kiko and Amara hold the ball together, facing camera | Medium hold |
| 3-6 sec | Both say: "Sharing is more fun!" with warm smiles | Medium hold |
| 6-9 sec | They give a small gentle wave to the camera | Medium hold |
| 9-12 sec | Warm smiles; the scene holds for a soft, gentle fade | Gentle pull-back |

## Sound

Soft playground ambience: birds, light breeze. Both voices together on the repeated phrase —
warm, sincere, and friendly. The ball is quiet in their hands. No music, no outro sting.
Natural ambience carries to the end.

## Emotion

Warm closure. The shared ball, the shared words, the shared wave — everything reinforces that
this is a friendship built on a simple, beautiful choice. The lesson is complete, and the
feeling is one of gentle accomplishment.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No competition, no lecture, no moralizing. The repeated phrase is delivered as a shared
discovery, not a rule being taught. The wave is friendly and inclusive — inviting the viewer
into the moment.

## Negative Prompt

low quality, blurry, deformed, extra limbs, text, watermark, photorealistic, horror, scary,
dark lighting, sharp playground equipment, metal playground, hard ground, falling, dangerous height,
crowd, competition, tug of war, grabbing, crying child, arguing faces, extra characters,
redesigned Benny's Playground, changed slide colour, missing ball pit, cinematic LUT, blue tint,
green tint, orange shift, HDR look, fast movement, sudden camera motion, static talking pose,
characters frozen, background music, music, melody, song, soundtrack, exaggerated wave, dramatic
fade, lesson-on-screen text, moralizing expression, adult voice-over, preachy tone

## QA Checklist

- [ ] Kiko + Amara identity preserved; final expressions warm and relaxed.
- [ ] Benny's Playground identity preserved: blue slide, ball pit, rounded equipment, soft grass.
- [ ] The purple ball is held jointly; continuity from Shot 07.
- [ ] "Sharing is more fun" delivered as shared discovery, not lecture.
- [ ] The wave is gentle and friendly; not exaggerated.
- [ ] No on-screen text; calm but alive; no frozen pose.
- [ ] The closing feels warm and complete — no loose ends.

#### BLD-EP08 — Shot 07 — Kiko's Pride (Relief)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP08 — Share and Play |
| Shot | 07 / 08 |
| Duration | 12 seconds |
| Location | Benny's Playground — Ball Pit Area |
| Characters | Kiko, Amara |
| Time of Day | Warm Morning |
| Spine step | RELIEF |

## Purpose

Kiko internalizes the sharing lesson — she voluntarily pushes the ball toward Amara, then they
bring it back together. Kiko feels proud and comfortable with her choice.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Kiko gently pushes the purple ball toward Amara — a deliberate, generous
gesture. This is the opposite of "It's mine" from Shot 02.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 06. The ball has been rolling in a gentle circle. Now Kiko
pushes it toward Amara, then they roll it back together. Background remains locked.

## Environment Anchors

- Same Benny's Playground Ball Pit Area; blue slide remains as landmark.
- `BP-BALLPIT-01` visible behind Kiko.
- The soft purple ball moves toward Amara, then back toward Kiko.
- Both characters are kneeling, relaxed and proud.
- No new props, no new characters, no background movement.

## Background Object Lock

Identical to Shots 01–06. Background locked from first frame. Only Kiko, Amara, and the
purple ball move. The ball pit, blue slide, grass, and rounded equipment remain stable.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Benny's Playground Ball Pit Area, warm morning. Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown pigtails) gently
pushes the soft purple ball toward Amara (yellow shirt, purple short overalls, yellow bow
headband, two dark brown puff buns). Amara receives it with a bright smile, then pushes it back.
Both characters are kneeling on the soft grass, relaxed and proud. Kiko's expression is warm and
confident — she chose to share, and it feels right. Soft pastel colours, warm light, rounded safe
playground shapes, no other characters, {style} {camera} {lighting}

The Benny's Playground background is locked from the first frame; keep the blue slide, ball pit,
soft grass and rounded equipment stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

Medium two-shot at child eye level. Camera follows the ball's gentle push toward Amara, then
back toward Kiko. A soft back-and-forth movement mirrors the sharing action. Steady and calm.

## Dialogue

No spoken dialogue. Only soft, happy sounds — gentle laughter, the ball's soft roll on grass.

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-3 sec | Kiko pushes the purple ball gently toward Amara | Medium, follows ball |
| 3-6 sec | Amara receives it, smiles, pushes it back toward Kiko | Medium, follows ball |
| 6-9 sec | Kiko catches it, pushes it back toward Amara again | Medium, follows ball |
| 9-12 sec | Both laugh softly; Kiko's face shows quiet pride | Medium hold on both |

## Sound

Soft playground ambience: birds, light breeze. The ball's soft rolling sound continues — a
gentle rhythm of push-and-return. Light, happy breathing. No dialogue, no music.

## Emotion

Kiko's internalization of the sharing lesson. The push-and-return is a physical metaphor for
generosity — giving and receiving in a gentle loop. Kiko's pride comes not from being praised,
but from discovering that sharing feels good on its own.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No competition, no scoring, no speed. The ball moves slowly and gently. Both characters'
movements are calm and deliberate — no fast pushes, no grabbing.

## Negative Prompt

low quality, blurry, deformed, extra limbs, text, watermark, photorealistic, horror, scary,
dark lighting, sharp playground equipment, metal playground, hard ground, falling, dangerous height,
crowd, competition, tug of war, grabbing, crying child, arguing faces, extra characters,
redesigned Benny's Playground, changed slide colour, missing ball pit, cinematic LUT, blue tint,
green tint, orange shift, HDR look, fast movement, sudden camera motion, static talking pose,
characters frozen, background music, music, melody, song, soundtrack, fast pushing, competitive
rally, scoring, speed, adult approval gesture, thumbs up from off-screen

## QA Checklist

- [ ] Kiko + Amara identity preserved; expressions match emotional beat.
- [ ] Benny's Playground identity preserved: blue slide, ball pit, rounded equipment, soft grass.
- [ ] The purple ball moves gently toward Amara and back; no fast pushing.
- [ ] Kiko's pride reads quiet and genuine; not boastful or performative.
- [ ] The sharing loop feels natural and cooperative.
- [ ] No competition, no scoring, no adult approval.
- [ ] No on-screen text; calm but alive; no frozen pose.

#### BLD-EP08 — Shot 06 — Sharing Is More Fun (Relief)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP08 — Share and Play |
| Shot | 06 / 08 |
| Duration | 15 seconds |
| Location | Benny's Playground — Ball Pit Area |
| Characters | Kiko, Amara |
| Time of Day | Warm Morning |
| Spine step | RELIEF |

## Purpose

The emotional payoff: Kiko and Amara realize that playing together with the ball is more fun
than playing alone. The repeated phrase "Sharing is more fun" is delivered naturally.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Both characters are still rolling the ball together, now laughing softly.
The joy is evident — sharing has created something better than solo play.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 05. The ball is still rolling in its gentle circle. Both
characters are now more relaxed, more expressive. Background remains locked.

## Environment Anchors

- Same Benny's Playground Ball Pit Area; blue slide remains as landmark.
- `BP-BALLPIT-01` visible behind Kiko.
- The soft purple ball continues its gentle circular roll on the grass.
- Both characters are kneeling, relaxed and happy.
- No new props, no new characters, no background movement.

## Background Object Lock

Identical to Shots 01–05. Background locked from first frame. Only Kiko, Amara, and the
purple ball move. The ball pit, blue slide, grass, and rounded equipment remain stable.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Benny's Playground Ball Pit Area, warm morning. Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown pigtails) and
Amara (yellow shirt, purple short overalls, yellow bow headband, two dark brown puff buns) kneel
on the soft grass, still rolling the soft purple ball together in its gentle circle. Both are
laughing softly — genuine, warm smiles. Kiko looks at Amara and says: "Sharing is more fun."
Amara nods, her eyes bright with joy. Soft pastel colours, warm light, rounded safe playground
shapes, no other characters, {style} {camera} {lighting}

The Benny's Playground background is locked from the first frame; keep the blue slide, ball pit,
soft grass and rounded equipment stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

Medium two-shot at child eye level, slightly wider to capture both characters' full expressions.
Camera holds steady, letting the natural joy breathe. A very gentle pull-back to show the
whole scene — two friends sharing a ball in a warm playground.

## Dialogue

```text
Kiko: Sharing is more fun.
Amara: Yeah!
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-3 sec | Both roll the ball together, laughing softly | Medium two-shot |
| 3-7 sec | Kiko looks at Amara and says: "Sharing is more fun" | Medium hold |
| 7-11 sec | Amara nods and smiles brightly; they continue rolling | Medium hold |
| 11-15 sec | Both laugh gently; the ball completes another soft circle | Gentle pull-back |

## Sound

Soft playground ambience: birds, light breeze. The ball's soft rolling sound continues. Light,
happy laughter from both children — natural, not forced. Kiko's voice is warm and genuine.
No music, no triumphant fanfare.

## Emotion

Pure relief and joy. The "more fun" realization is organic — not preached, but felt. Kiko
discovers that sharing didn't take anything away; it added something. Amara's bright response
validates the discovery.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No competition, no comparison to solo play, no lecture. The joy is in the moment — two
children laughing together over a simple shared activity.

## Negative Prompt

low quality, blurry, deformed, extra limbs, text, watermark, photorealistic, horror, scary,
dark lighting, sharp playground equipment, metal playground, hard ground, falling, dangerous height,
crowd, competition, tug of war, grabbing, crying child, arguing faces, extra characters,
redesigned Benny's Playground, changed slide colour, missing ball pit, cinematic LUT, blue tint,
green tint, orange shift, HDR look, fast movement, sudden camera motion, static talking pose,
characters frozen, background music, music, melody, song, soundtrack, exaggerated laughter,
over-the-top joy, competitive victory, scoreboard, winner/loser visual

## QA Checklist

- [ ] Kiko + Amara identity preserved; expressions match emotional beat.
- [ ] Benny's Playground identity preserved: blue slide, ball pit, rounded equipment, soft grass.
- [ ] The purple ball continues rolling; continuity from Shot 05.
- [ ] "Sharing is more fun" delivered naturally; not forced or preachy.
- [ ] Both characters' joy reads genuine and warm.
- [ ] No competition, no comparison, no lecture.
- [ ] No on-screen text; calm but alive; no frozen pose.

#### BLD-EP08 — Shot 05 — Rolling Together (Action)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP08 — Share and Play |
| Shot | 05 / 08 |
| Duration | 15 seconds |
| Location | Benny's Playground — Ball Pit Area |
| Characters | Kiko, Amara |
| Time of Day | Warm Morning |
| Spine step | ACTION |

## Purpose

Show the core sharing activity: Kiko and Amara roll the ball together in a small circle on the
ground — not passing it back and forth, but guiding it jointly. This defines the episode's
unique approach to sharing.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Both characters kneel beside the ball. Their hands hover near it but don't
grab — they're about to start a shared activity.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 04. The purple ball is on the grass between them. Now both
characters kneel and begin rolling it together. Background remains locked.

## Environment Anchors

- Same Benny's Playground Ball Pit Area; blue slide remains as landmark.
- `BP-BALLPIT-01` visible behind Kiko.
- The soft purple ball is on the soft grass between Kiko and Amara.
- Both characters are now kneeling at child eye level.
- No new props, no new characters, no background movement.

## Background Object Lock

Identical to Shots 01–04. Background locked from first frame. Only Kiko, Amara, and the
purple ball move. The ball pit, blue slide, grass, and rounded equipment remain stable.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Benny's Playground Ball Pit Area, warm morning. Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown pigtails) and
Amara (yellow shirt, purple short overalls, yellow bow headband, two dark brown puff buns) kneel
on the soft grass facing each other. Between them, the soft purple playground ball rolls slowly
in a small gentle circle on the grass — guided by both of their hands moving together, not
passing it back and forth. Both children smile as they guide the ball in its soft circular path.
Soft pastel colours, warm light, rounded safe playground shapes, no other characters, {style}
{camera} {lighting}

The Benny's Playground background is locked from the first frame; keep the blue slide, ball pit,
soft grass and rounded equipment stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

Low-angle medium shot at child eye level, both characters and the ball visible. Camera holds
steady as the ball rolls in its small circle. A very gentle orbit movement follows the ball's
circular path — subtle, not dizzying.

## Dialogue

```text
Kiko: Let's roll it together!
Amara: Yeah!
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-3 sec | Kiko and Amara kneel on either side of the ball | Low medium hold |
| 3-7 sec | Both guide the ball gently in a small circle on the grass | Gentle orbit |
| 7-11 sec | The ball completes one slow circle; both smile | Orbit holds |
| 11-15 sec | They guide it for another gentle circle; natural laughter | Steady medium |

## Sound

Soft playground ambience: birds, light breeze. The ball makes a very soft rolling sound on
the grass — a gentle whoosh-whoosh as it circles. Light, happy breathing from both children.
No music, no competitive sound, no bouncing.

## Emotion

Pure shared joy. The circular rolling is a cooperative act — neither child dominates, neither
waits for a turn. They're doing the same thing at the same time, and it feels good. This is
the heart of the episode's message: sharing means doing something together.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No competition, no turn-taking pressure, no grabbing. Both hands guide the ball gently. The
circular motion is slow and soft — no fast rolling, no chasing, no ball escaping.

## Negative Prompt

low quality, blurry, deformed, extra limbs, text, watermark, photorealistic, horror, scary,
dark lighting, sharp playground equipment, metal playground, hard ground, falling, dangerous height,
crowd, competition, tug of war, grabbing, crying child, arguing faces, extra characters,
redesigned Benny's Playground, changed slide colour, missing ball pit, cinematic LUT, blue tint,
green tint, orange shift, HDR look, fast movement, sudden camera motion, static talking pose,
characters frozen, background music, music, melody, song, soundtrack, fast rolling, chasing ball,
ball escaping, pushing, shoving, turn-taking visual, waiting in line, competitive expression

## QA Checklist

- [ ] Kiko + Amara identity preserved; expressions match emotional beat.
- [ ] Benny's Playground identity preserved: blue slide, ball pit, rounded equipment, soft grass.
- [ ] The purple ball rolls in a small circle; not passed back and forth.
- [ ] Both characters guide the ball together; neither dominates.
- [ ] The rolling is slow, soft, and cooperative.
- [ ] No competition, no turn-taking, no chasing, no fast movement.
- [ ] No on-screen text; calm but alive; no frozen pose.

#### BLD-EP08 — Shot 04 — You Can Play Too (Action)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP08 — Share and Play |
| Shot | 04 / 08 |
| Duration | 12 seconds |
| Location | Benny's Playground — Ball Pit Area |
| Characters | Kiko, Amara |
| Time of Day | Warm Morning |
| Spine step | ACTION |

## Purpose

Kiko makes the first sharing move — she lowers the ball from her chest and places it between
herself and Amara. This is the physical commitment to sharing.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Kiko looks at the ball in her arms, then slowly lowers it. The movement
is deliberate and gentle — a choice, not a surrender.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 03. Kiko has just seen Amara's face and paused. Now she acts.
The background remains locked. The purple ball moves from Kiko's chest to the space between
the two characters.

## Environment Anchors

- Same Benny's Playground Ball Pit Area; blue slide remains as landmark.
- `BP-BALLPIT-01` visible behind Kiko.
- The soft purple ball moves from Kiko's arms to the ground between them.
- Amara stands a small step away, watching Kiko's movement.
- No new props, no new characters, no background movement.

## Background Object Lock

Identical to Shots 01–03. Background locked from first frame. Only Kiko, Amara, and the
purple ball move. The ball pit, blue slide, grass, and rounded equipment remain stable.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Benny's Playground Ball Pit Area, warm morning. Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown pigtails) slowly
lowers the soft purple ball from her chest and places it gently on the soft grass between herself
and Amara. Her expression shifts from possessive to开放. She says: "You can play too." Amara
(yellow shirt, purple short overalls, yellow bow headband, two dark brown puff buns) watches
the ball land between them, her smile returning. Soft pastel colours, warm light, rounded safe
playground shapes, no other characters, {style} {camera} {lighting}

The Benny's Playground background is locked from the first frame; keep the blue slide, ball pit,
soft grass and rounded equipment stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

Medium shot, both characters visible. Camera follows the ball's gentle descent from Kiko's
arms to the ground. A soft tilt down as the ball lands, then back up to both faces. Steady,
calm movement.

## Dialogue

```text
Kiko: You can play too.
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-3 sec | Kiko looks at the ball, then begins to lower it | Medium hold |
| 3-6 sec | The ball descends gently from Kiko's chest toward the grass | Tilt down with ball |
| 6-9 sec | The ball settles on the soft grass between them; Kiko's hands release it | Tilt holds on ball |
| 9-12 sec | Kiko looks at Amara: "You can play too." Amara's smile returns | Tilt up to faces |

## Sound

Soft playground ambience: birds, light breeze. A very gentle thud as the ball touches soft
grass — almost inaudible. Kiko's voice is warm and sincere. No music, no triumphant sting.

## Emotion

The first act of sharing — quiet, genuine, and self-directed. Kiko isn't told to share; she
chooses to. The ball's gentle descent mirrors her emotional opening. Amara's returning smile
validates the choice.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No forced sharing, no adult intervention, no guilt. Kiko's action is voluntary and natural.
The ball is placed gently — not thrown, not pushed, not handed reluctantly.

## Negative Prompt

low quality, blurry, deformed, extra limbs, text, watermark, photorealistic, horror, scary,
dark lighting, sharp playground equipment, metal playground, hard ground, falling, dangerous height,
crowd, competition, tug of war, grabbing, crying child, arguing faces, extra characters,
redesigned Benny's Playground, changed slide colour, missing ball pit, cinematic LUT, blue tint,
green tint, orange shift, HDR look, fast movement, sudden camera motion, static talking pose,
characters frozen, background music, music, melody, song, soundtrack, forced gesture,reluctant handover, adult hand in frame, guilt expression, dramatic release

## QA Checklist

- [ ] Kiko + Amara identity preserved; expressions match emotional beat.
- [ ] Benny's Playground identity preserved: blue slide, ball pit, rounded equipment, soft grass.
- [ ] The purple ball moves smoothly from Kiko's arms to the ground between them.
- [ ] Kiko's sharing reads as a genuine choice; not forced or reluctant.
- [ ] Amara's smile returns naturally; not exaggerated.
- [ ] No adult hands, no external intervention, no guilt.
- [ ] No on-screen text; calm but alive; no frozen pose.

#### BLD-EP08 — Shot 03 — Can I Play Too? (Support)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP08 — Share and Play |
| Shot | 03 / 08 |
| Duration | 15 seconds |
| Location | Benny's Playground — Ball Pit Area |
| Characters | Kiko, Amara |
| Time of Day | Warm Morning |
| Spine step | SUPPORT |

## Purpose

The emotional turning point: Amara asks gently, and Kiko pauses to really see Amara's face.
This shot bridges the "mine" feeling to the "maybe we can share" realization.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Amara takes a small step closer and speaks softly. The camera catches both
characters in the same frame — the distance between them is small but meaningful.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 02. Kiko is still holding the purple ball. Amara's smile has

## BLD-EP09 — "I'm Sorry" (viewing #9)

- **Tema:** Özür dileme · **Mekan:** Central Square / Kiko's Home · **Kadro:** Kiko, Arda
- **Repeated phrase:** "I'm sorry. Are you okay?"
- **Spine:** (1) Kiko yanlışlıkla Arda'nın blok kulesini devirir. (2) Arda üzülür. (3) Kiko kötü hisseder,
  ne yapacağını bilemez. (4) Kiko "I'm sorry. Are you okay?" der, yardım eder. (5) Birlikte tekrar yaparlar.
  (6) Arda gülümser. (7) Barışırlar. (8) Özür dilemek dostluğu onarır.
- **Not:** Kaza küçük ve masum (kötü niyet yok). Yeni canon yok.

### Scene Definition Starter

- **Kapsam kararı:** Tek ana set olarak **Central Square — Big Pompom Tree çevresi** kullanılır.
  Kiko's Home alternatif mekan olarak kalır; üretimde mekan geçişi açılmaz.
- **Prop:** Önceden üretimde kullanılan soft rounded building blocks diline uyumlu, **tam 8 yumuşak blok**.
  Bloklar oyuncak prop olarak shot içinde seed edilir; yeni dünya canon'u oluşturmaz.
- **Safe-exposure:** Kule devrilmesi "crash" değil, yumuşak "soft topple"dır. Arda'nın üzülmesi küçük
  bir yüz düşmesi/omuz düşmesidir; ağlama krizi yok, suçlama yok.

| Shot | Spine | Scene amacı | Kısa tanım |
|---:|---|---|---|
| 01 | Problem | Oyunu kur | Kiko ve Arda Central Square'de sekiz yumuşak blokla küçük bir kule yapar. |
| 02 | Problem | Küçük kaza | Kiko bir bloğa uzanırken kuleye hafifçe değer; kule yumuşakça dağılır. |
| 03 | Feeling | Duyguyu göster | Arda'nın gülümsemesi düşer; Kiko durur ve "Uh-oh" hissini yaşar. |
| 04 | Support | Özür cümlesi | Kiko yaklaşır: "I'm sorry. Are you okay?" |
| 05 | Action | Onarmaya başlama | Kiko Arda'yla birlikte blokları toplar; aynı 8 blok korunur. |
| 06 | Action | Birlikte yeniden yapma | Kuleyi bu kez daha alçak ve sağlam yaparlar. |
| 07 | Relief | Barışma | Arda gülümser; Kiko rahatlar. "I'm sorry. Are you okay?" sıcakça tekrarlanır. |
| 08 | Lesson | Sıcak kapanış | İkisi minik kule yanında el sallar; hata olunca özür ve yardım dostluğu onarır. |

#### BLD-EP09 — Shot 03 — The Feeling (Feeling)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP09 — I'm Sorry |
| Shot | 03 / 08 |
| Duration | 12 seconds |

creates the opening for an apology.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Arda's face in close-up — his smile slowly drops as he sees the scattered
blocks. A small, soft sadness. The world pauses.

the grass. Background remains locked from Shot 01.

```text
Kiko: Uh-oh.
```

## Shot Breakdown

|---|---|---|

| 6-9 sec | Both look at the scattered blocks; a quiet pause | Wide two-shot |
| 9-12 sec | Kiko sits still, thinking; face shows "I feel bad" | Medium hold on Kiko |

## Sound

A quiet moment — playground ambience drops to near silence. No block sounds. The world
pauses around the two characters. Natural ambience at its softest.

## Emotion

Arda feels a small sadness (a soft face-drop, a soft shoulder-drop), and Kiko feels the
"Uh-oh" — but no crying meltdown, no blame. Both freeze: "What should I do?" This moment
creates the ground for an apology.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No crying meltdown, no blame, no scolding, no angry faces, no shouting, no finger pointing.
Arda's sadness is a small facial shift — not tears, not withdrawal. Kiko's reaction is
surprise and mild guilt, not panic.

## Negative Prompt

dark lighting, sharp blocks, metal blocks, hard ground, falling, dangerous height, crowd,

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP09 — I'm Sorry |
| Shot | 04 / 08 |
| Duration | 12 seconds |

is deliberate — she's choosing to apologize, not being told to.

## BLD-EP10 — "Thank You!" (viewing #10)

- **Tema:** Teşekkür etme · **Mekan:** Central Square · **Kadro:** Kiko, Mimi (+ kısa bir yardımcı figür)
- **Repeated phrase:** "Thank you!"
- **Spine:** (1) Kiko bir şeyini düşürür / uzanamaz. (2) Küçük bir zorluk. (3) Biri (Mimi/komşu) yardım eder.
  (4) Kiko "Thank you!" der. (5) İçini sıcaklık kaplar. (6) O da başkasına yardım edip teşekkür alır.
  (7) Teşekkür zinciri. (8) "Thank you!" ile kapanış.
- **Not:** Yeni canon yok.

### Scene Definition Starter

- **Kapsam kararı:** Tek ana set olarak **Central Square — Big Pompom Tree çevresi** kullanılır.
  Kısa yardımcı figür yerine **Mimi** kullanılır; konuşan karakter sayısı 2'de kalır.
- **Prop:** Tek yumuşak sarı top. Top, S01E10'daki "turn-taking" yapısına girmeden yalnızca
  yardım/teşekkür nesnesi olarak kullanılır.
- **Çakışma önleme:** Bu bölüm "topu sırayla oynamak" değil, **yardım görünce teşekkür etmek ve
  sonra yardım etmeyi fark etmek** üzerinedir.

| Shot | Spine | Scene amacı | Kısa tanım |
|---:|---|---|---|
| 01 | Problem | Küçük zorluk | Kiko'nun yumuşak sarı topu, Big Pompom Tree köklerinin yanına yavaşça yuvarlanır. |
| 02 | Feeling | Yardıma ihtiyaç | Kiko uzanır ama yetişemez; "Oh no." der, sakin kalır. |
| 03 | Support | Mimi yardım eder | Mimi topu nazikçe geri iter. |
| 04 | Action | Teşekkür | Kiko gülümser: "Thank you!" |
| 05 | Relief | Sıcaklık | Mimi mutlu olur; Kiko teşekkürün iyi hissettirdiğini fark eder. |
| 06 | Action | Kiko yardım eder | Mimi topu taşırken zorlanır; Kiko birlikte taşımayı teklif eder. |
| 07 | Relief | Teşekkür zinciri | Mimi: "Thank you!" Kiko gülümser. |
| 08 | Lesson | Sıcak kapanış | Kiko ve Mimi topu birlikte tutar; "Thank you!" ile kapanır. |

#### BLD-EP10 — Shot 01 — The Rolling Ball (Problem)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP10 — Thank You! |
| Shot | 01 / 08 |
| Duration | 15 seconds |
| Location | Central Square — Big Pompom Tree area |

| Time of Day | Warm Morning |
| Spine step | PROBLEM |

## Purpose

Open with a simple, readable need: Kiko's soft yellow ball rolls slowly toward the Big Pompom
Tree roots and stops just out of reach. This creates a gentle problem that naturally invites
help from a friend.

## Opening Hook

First 3–5 seconds: The soft yellow ball rolls gently across the warm morning grass and comes
to rest near the tree roots. The movement is slow, safe, and instantly readable — a ball that
needs retrieving.

## Continuity

First story shot, after the shared Brave Little Days opening bumper. This shot establishes the
Central Square setting, the two characters, and the ball. Background: Big Pompom Tree visible,
soft grass, warm morning light.

## Environment Anchors

- Central Square, soft grass near Big Pompom Tree.
- One soft yellow ball rolling slowly across the grass.
- Big Pompom Tree with visible roots as natural resting point.
- No other characters, no background movement, no hard surfaces.

## Background Object Lock

Kiko, Mimi, and the single soft yellow ball move.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Central Square near Big Pompom Tree, warm morning. One soft yellow playground ball rolls slowly
across the soft green grass toward the tree roots. Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown pigtails)
watches the ball roll with a surprised expression: "Oh, my ball!" Mimi (purple shirt, light
pink skirt, two hair buns) stands nearby, looking ready to help. Big Pompom Tree visible,
soft green grass, rounded safe shapes, no other characters, {style} {camera} {lighting}

The Central Square background is locked from the first frame; keep Big Pompom Tree, soft grass
and rounded shapes stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

32mm wide at child eye level establishing Central Square and Big Pompom Tree; slow settle to
medium on Kiko, Mimi, and the rolling yellow ball. Stable settle only.

## Dialogue

```text

Mimi: I can help.
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-4 sec | Central Square visible; the soft yellow ball rolls gently across grass | Wide |
| 4-8 sec | Kiko notices the ball: "Oh, my ball!" | Settle |
| 8-12 sec | Mimi steps closer, ready to help | Medium |
| 12-15 sec | The ball stops near the tree roots; Mimi says: "I can help" | Medium hold |

## Sound

Soft playground ambience: birds, light breeze. The ball makes a very gentle rolling sound on
the grass. Natural ambience only. No music, no loud bounce, no competitive play sound.

## Emotion

Warm curiosity and the beginning of a small help moment. No conflict yet; the feeling is light
and friendly. Kiko's "Oh, my ball!" is surprised but calm — not panicked.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No chase, no fast roll, no competition, no extra characters. The ball rolls slowly and stops
naturally. Mimi's offer to help is gentle and unsolicited — no prompting needed.

## Negative Prompt

low quality, blurry, deformed, extra limbs, text, watermark, photorealistic, horror, scary,
dark lighting, sharp equipment, metal surfaces, hard ground, falling, dangerous height, crowd,
competition, chase, fast roll, hiding under hard objects, extra helper, thank-you song,

motion, static talking pose, characters frozen, background music, music, melody, song, soundtrack

- [ ] Central Square identity preserved: Big Pompom Tree, soft grass, rounded shapes.
- [ ] The yellow ball is soft, round and safe; no hard bounce or fast movement.
- [ ] Help setup reads mild and friendly; no conflict escalation.
- [ ] No on-screen text; calm but alive; no frozen pose.

#### BLD-EP10 — Shot 02 — Reaching (Feeling)

## Scene Context

|---|---|

| Shot | 02 / 08 |

## Purpose

This is a gentle, age-appropriate difficulty that establishes the need for help without drama.

## Opening Hook

is close but not quite touchable — nestled between soft roots. The effort is natural and calm.

- Mimi stands nearby, watching.
- No other characters, no background movement.

#### BLD-EP10 — Shot 03 — Mimi Helps (Support)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|

#### BLD-EP10 — Shot 04 — Thank You! (Action)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|

| Shot | 04 / 08 |
| Duration | 12 seconds |
| Location | Central Square — Big Pompom Tree area |

| Time of Day | Warm Morning |
| Spine step | ACTION |

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Kiko looks at the ball at her feet, then turns to Mimi with a bright,
sincere smile. The gratitude is visible before the words come.

- No other characters, no background movement.

karşılık. Playground ambience devam eder — kuşlar, hafif rüzgar.

#### BLD-EP10 — Shot 05 — Warm Feeling (Relief)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP10 — Thank You! |
| Shot | 05 / 08 |
| Duration | 12 seconds |
| Location | Central Square — Big Pompom Tree area |
| Characters | Kiko, Mimi |
| Time of Day | Warm Morning |
| Spine step | RELIEF |

## Purpose

Show the emotional payoff: Mimi responds with "You're welcome!" and both characters feel the
warmth of the gratitude exchange. Kiko begins to understand that thanking someone makes both
people feel good.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Mimi responds to Kiko's "Thank you!" with a bright "You're welcome!" — her
face is warm and happy. The reciprocal feeling is immediate and genuine.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 04. Kiko has just said "Thank you!" Now Mimi responds, and the
emotional warmth settles in. Background remains locked.

## Environment Anchors

- Same Central Square location; Big Pompom Tree visible.
- One soft yellow ball at Kiko's feet, held gently.
- Both characters face each other with warm expressions.
- No other characters, no background movement.

## Background Object Lock

Identical to Shots 01–04. Background locked from first frame. Only Kiko and Mimi move.
The tree, grass, and rounded shapes remain stable.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Central Square near Big Pompom Tree, warm morning. Mimi (purple shirt, light pink skirt, two
hair buns) responds with a bright, warm smile: "You're welcome!" Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown
pigtails) holds the soft yellow ball gently, feeling the warmth of the exchange. Both characters
face each other with genuine happiness. Big Pompom Tree visible, soft green grass, rounded safe
shapes, no other characters, {style} {camera} {lighting}

The Central Square background is locked from the first frame; keep Big Pompom Tree, soft grass
and rounded shapes stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

Close-up on Mimi's response, then a gentle pull-back to show both characters in a warm two-shot.
Steady framing, letting the emotional warmth breathe.

## Dialogue

```text
Mimi: You're welcome!
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-3 sec | Mimi responds with a bright smile: "You're welcome!" | Close-up on Mimi |
| 3-6 sec | Kiko holds the ball, feeling the warmth | Medium on Kiko |
| 6-9 sec | Kiko realizes that thanking feels good — a soft, genuine smile | Close-up on Kiko |
| 9-12 sec | Both characters rest in a warm, comfortable silence | Two-shot hold |

## Sound

Nazik bir "You're welcome!" karşılığı. Sıcak, samimi ses tonları. Playground ambience devam
eder — kuşlar, hafif rüzgar. Sessiz bir an.

## Emotion

Warmth — thanking and being thanked both feel good. Kiko begins to understand the cycle:
help → thank → both feel warm. This is the emotional seed that will grow into the thank-you
chain later in the episode.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No competition, no comparison, no "now you owe me" undertone, no adult intervention. The
warmth is mutual and natural — not transactional.

## Negative Prompt

low quality, blurry, deformed, extra limbs, text, watermark, photorealistic, horror, scary,
dark lighting, sharp equipment, metal surfaces, hard ground, falling, dangerous height, crowd,
competition, "now you owe me" undertone, adult intervention, dramatic music, lesson recitation,
cinematic LUT, blue tint, green tint, orange shift, HDR look, fast movement, sudden camera
motion, static talking pose, characters frozen, background music, music, melody, song, soundtrack

## QA Checklist

- [ ] Kiko + Mimi identity preserved; expressions match emotional beat.
- [ ] Central Square identity preserved: Big Pompom Tree, soft grass, rounded shapes.
- [ ] The warmth of the gratitude exchange reads genuine and mutual.
- [ ] Mimi's "You're welcome!" is bright and warm; not dismissive.
- [ ] No on-screen text; calm but alive; no frozen pose.

#### BLD-EP10 — Shot 06 — Kiko Helps Back (Action)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP10 — Thank You! |
| Shot | 06 / 08 |
| Duration | 12 seconds |
| Location | Central Square — Big Pompom Tree area |
| Characters | Kiko, Mimi |
| Time of Day | Warm Morning |
| Spine step | ACTION |

## Purpose

The thank-you chain begins: Mimi now needs help, and Kiko offers to carry the ball together.
This reverses the roles — the helper becomes the helped, and the helped becomes the helper.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Mimi tries to carry the ball; it's a little big for her and she wobbles
slightly. Kiko notices immediately and steps in to help.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 05. The ball is now being moved by Mimi. Kiko, having just been
helped, now sees Mimi struggling and offers her help. Background remains locked.

## Environment Anchors

- Same Central Square location; Big Pompom Tree visible.
- One soft yellow ball being carried by Mimi, slightly wobbly.
- Kiko steps in to help carry the ball.
- No other characters, no background movement.

## Background Object Lock

Identical to Shots 01–05. Background locked from first frame. Only Kiko, Mimi, and the
yellow ball move. The tree, grass, and rounded shapes remain stable.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Central Square near Big Pompom Tree, warm morning. Mimi (purple shirt, light pink skirt, two
hair buns) carries the soft yellow ball with both arms; it's a little big and she wobbles
slightly. Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown pigtails) steps in and says: "Let's carry it together!"
Both characters hold the ball together and walk side by side. Big Pompom Tree visible, soft
green grass, rounded safe shapes, no other characters, {style} {camera} {lighting}

The Central Square background is locked from the first frame; keep Big Pompom Tree, soft grass
and rounded shapes stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

Medium shot following Mimi as she carries the ball, then widens to include Kiko stepping in.
Gentle tracking as both characters walk together holding the ball. Steady, warm framing.

## Dialogue

```text
Kiko: Let's carry it together!
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-3 sec | Mimi carries the ball; it's a little big, she wobbles | Medium on Mimi |
| 3-6 sec | Kiko steps in: "Let's carry it together!" | Medium two-shot |
| 6-9 sec | Both characters hold the ball together; walk side by side | Tracking, follows them |
| 9-12 sec | They walk together, the ball secure between them | Wide two-shot |

## Sound

Nazik bir "Let's carry it together!" teklifi. Topun yumuşak dokunuş sesi — iki çocuğun
birlikte taşıması. Playground ambience devam eder.

## Emotion

The help cycle reverses — Kiko, who was helped, now helps back. The thank-you chain begins
naturally. This is the episode's second key beat: gratitude leads to reciprocal kindness.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No heavy lifting, no struggle, no "I can do it myself" refusal from Mimi, no competition, no
speed, no rushing. The carrying is gentle and cooperative.

## Negative Prompt

low quality, blurry, deformed, extra limbs, text, watermark, photorealistic, horror, scary,
dark lighting, sharp equipment, metal surfaces, hard ground, falling, dangerous height, crowd,
competition, heavy lifting, struggle, "I can do it myself" refusal, rushing, speed, cinematic
LUT, blue tint, green tint, orange shift, HDR look, fast movement, sudden camera motion, static
talking pose, characters frozen, background music, music, melody, song, soundtrack

## QA Checklist

- [ ] Kiko + Mimi identity preserved; expressions match emotional beat.
- [ ] Central Square identity preserved: Big Pompom Tree, soft grass, rounded shapes.
- [ ] The yellow ball is carried together; not too heavy, not dropped.
- [ ] Kiko's help reads natural and willing; not forced.
- [ ] The role reversal (helper becomes helped) is clear but subtle.
- [ ] No on-screen text; calm but alive; no frozen pose.

#### BLD-EP10 — Shot 07 — The Thank-You Chain (Relief)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |

## Opening Hook

#### BLD-EP10 — Shot 08 — Warm Closing (Lesson)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP10 — Thank You! |
| Shot | 08 / 08 |
| Duration | 12 seconds |
| Location | Central Square — Big Pompom Tree area |
| Characters | Kiko, Mimi |
| Time of Day | Warm Morning |
| Spine step | LESSON |

## Purpose

The warm closing shot: Kiko and Mimi hold the ball together and give a small wave to the
camera. The repeated phrase "Thank you!" is delivered one final time, sealing the lesson with
a friendly goodbye.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Both characters hold the yellow ball together between them, standing on
the warm grass. They look at the camera with warm, relaxed smiles.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 07. The ball has been carried together, the thank-you chain
is complete. Now they hold it together for a final shared moment. Background remains locked.

## Environment Anchors

- Same Central Square location; Big Pompom Tree visible.
- One soft yellow ball held jointly between Kiko and Mimi.
- Both characters standing, facing the camera.
- No new props, no new characters, no background movement.

## Background Object Lock

Identical to Shots 01–07. Background locked from first frame. Only Kiko and Mimi move.
The tree, grass, and rounded shapes remain stable.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Central Square near Big Pompom Tree, warm morning. Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown pigtails) and
Mimi (purple shirt, light pink skirt, two hair buns) stand together, holding the soft yellow
ball between them. Both face the camera with warm, relaxed smiles. They say: "Thank you!" Then
they give a small gentle wave. Soft pastel colours, warm light, rounded safe shapes, no other
characters, {style} {camera} {lighting}

The Central Square background is locked from the first frame; keep Big Pompom Tree, soft grass
and rounded shapes stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

Medium shot at child eye level, both characters centered in frame. Camera holds steady for the
final moment. A very gentle, almost imperceptible pull-back to show the full warm scene. The
shot fades to soft warmth at the end.

## Dialogue

```text
Kiko & Mimi: Thank you!
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-3 sec | Kiko and Mimi hold the ball together, facing camera | Medium hold |
| 3-6 sec | Both say: "Thank you!" with warm smiles | Medium hold |
| 6-9 sec | They give a small gentle wave to the camera | Medium hold |
| 9-12 sec | Warm smiles; the scene holds for a soft, gentle fade | Gentle pull-back |

## Sound

Sıcak, samimi ses tonları — birlikte söylenen "Thank you!" Playground ambience devam eder.
Nazik bir kapanış hissi. No music, no outro sting. Natural ambience carries to the end.

## Emotion

Warm closure. The shared ball, the shared words, the shared wave — everything reinforces that
gratitude strengthens friendship. The lesson is complete, and the feeling is one of gentle
accomplishment.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No competition, no lecture, no moralizing. The repeated phrase is delivered as a shared
discovery, not a rule being taught. The wave is friendly and inclusive — inviting the viewer
into the moment.

## Negative Prompt

low quality, blurry, deformed, extra limbs, text, watermark, photorealistic, horror, scary,
dark lighting, sharp equipment, metal surfaces, hard ground, falling, dangerous height, crowd,
competition, tug of war, grabbing, crying child, arguing faces, extra characters, cinematic LUT,
blue tint, green tint, orange shift, HDR look, fast movement, sudden camera motion, static
talking pose, characters frozen, background music, music, melody, song, soundtrack, exaggerated
wave, dramatic fade, lesson-on-screen text, moralizing expression, adult voice-over, preachy
tone

## QA Checklist

- [ ] Kiko + Mimi identity preserved; final expressions warm and relaxed.
- [ ] Central Square identity preserved: Big Pompom Tree, soft grass, rounded shapes.
- [ ] The yellow ball is held jointly; continuity from Shot 07.
- [ ] "Thank you!" delivered as shared discovery, not lecture.
- [ ] The wave is gentle and friendly; not exaggerated.
- [ ] No on-screen text; calm but alive; no frozen pose.
- [ ] The closing feels warm and complete — no loose ends.

## BLD-EP11 — "Slow Breaths" (viewing #11)

- **Tema:** Nefes alarak sakinleşme · **Mekan:** Opa's Tree / Kiko's Home · **Kadro:** Kiko, Opa
- **Repeated phrase:** "Breathe in, breathe out."
- **Spine:** (1) Kiko bir şeyle uğraşır (puzzle uymuyor). (2) Sinirlenmeye başlar. (3) Opa nazikçe gelir,
  "Let's breathe." (4) Birlikte yavaş nefes (çiçeği kokla, mumu üfle). (5) Kiko sakinleşir. (6) Tekrar dener.
  (7) Başarır. (8) "Breathe in, breathe out." — kızınca sakinleşmeyi öğrenmek.
- **Not:** EP12 ile bağlantılı (öfke yönetimi). Yeni canon yok.

### Scene Definition Starter

- **Kapsam kararı:** Tek ana set olarak **Kiko's Home — Living Room / toy rug** kullanılır.
  Opa's Tree bu bölüm için atmosferik alternatif olarak kalır; Opa, Kiko's Home'a nazikçe ziyaret eder.
- **Prop:** `KH-TOYBOX-01` çevresinden çıkan basit, yumuşak **round puzzle**. Puzzle parçası
  bir an uymuyor; parça keskin değil, küçük boğulma riski gibi okunmayacak kadar büyük.
- **Safe-exposure:** "Kızgınlık" görseli yoğun öfke değildir; Kiko'nun kaşları hafifçe büzülür,
  omuzları gerilir, sonra nefesle yumuşar. Candle/fire yok; "mumu üfle" yerine hayali "pompom puff"
  veya çiçek koklama metaforu kullanılır.

| Shot | Spine | Scene amacı | Kısa tanım |
|---:|---|---|---|
| 01 | Problem | Puzzle zorluğu | Kiko yuvarlak halıda büyük bir puzzle parçasını yerine oturtmaya çalışır. |
| 02 | Feeling | Büyük duygu | Parça uymayınca Kiko durur: "It won't fit." |
| 03 | Support | Opa yaklaşır | Opa sakin gelir: "Let's breathe." |
| 04 | Action | Nefes modeli | Opa ve Kiko çiçeği koklar gibi nefes alır, pompom puff üfler gibi nefes verir. |
| 05 | Relief | Beden yumuşar | Kiko'nun omuzları iner; yüzü rahatlar. |
| 06 | Action | Yeniden deneme | Kiko puzzle parçasını çevirip tekrar dener. |
| 07 | Relief | Başarı | Parça yerine oturur; Kiko küçük bir gülümseme verir. |
| 08 | Lesson | Sıcak kapanış | Kiko ve Opa: "Breathe in, breathe out." |

#### BLD-EP11 — Shot 01 — The Puzzle Piece (Problem)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP11 — Slow Breaths |
| Shot | 01 / 08 |
| Duration | 15 seconds |
| Location | Kiko's Home — Living Room / toy rug |
| Characters | Kiko, Opa |
| Time of Day | Warm Daytime |
| Spine step | PROBLEM |

## Purpose

Open with a gentle puzzle challenge: Kiko tries to place a large soft puzzle piece into its
slot on a round puzzle board. The piece doesn't quite fit — it's slightly turned the wrong way.
The problem is real but calm; frustration hasn't arrived yet.

## Opening Hook

First 3–5 seconds: Kiko sits on the soft toy rug, holding a large soft round puzzle piece above
a matching round puzzle board. The piece is almost right but tilted. The object is instantly
readable, safe, and inviting.

## Continuity

First story shot, after the shared Brave Little Days opening bumper. This shot's approved
first-frame still = **Episode Colour Master**. Maintain Kiko + Opa identity, Kiko's Home
living room world identity, warm daytime light. Do not redesign the room.

## Environment Anchors

- Kiko's Home — Living Room; soft toy rug on the floor, warm daytime light.
- One large soft round puzzle board (bright pastel colours, safe rounded edges).
- One large soft round puzzle piece in Kiko's hands.
- Opa nearby, sitting or kneeling at child eye level, warm and present.
- No new props, no extra characters, no background movement.

## Background Object Lock

Background locked from first frame. Keep the soft toy rug, living room walls, warm daylight
stable. Only Kiko, Opa, and the puzzle pieces move.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Kiko's Home Living Room, warm daytime. Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown pigtails) sits on a soft
toy rug, holding a large soft round puzzle piece above a matching round puzzle board. The piece
is slightly tilted — almost right but not quite fitting. Opa (warm grey sweater, soft features,
gentle eyes) sits nearby at child eye level, watching calmly. Soft pastel colours, warm
daylight, rounded safe shapes, cozy living room, no other characters, {style} {camera} {lighting}

The Kiko's Home background is locked from the first frame; keep the soft toy rug, warm daylight
and cozy living room stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

Medium shot at child eye level, Kiko and the puzzle board centered. Slow settle to medium on
Kiko's hands and the piece. Stable settle only. No fast cuts, no dramatic angles.

## Dialogue

```text
Kiko: It won't fit.

Opa: Take your time.
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-4 sec | Kiko sits on toy rug, holds large puzzle piece over the board | Medium |
| 4-8 sec | She tries to place it; it doesn't quite fit — slightly tilted | Settle on hands |
| 8-12 sec | Kiko pauses, looks at the piece: "It won't fit." | Medium on Kiko |
| 12-15 sec | Opa watches calmly: "Take your time." | Medium two-shot |

## Sound

Soft toy rug ambience — cozy indoor quiet. The puzzle piece makes a gentle "pof" sound as it
touches the board. Kiko's voice shows mild frustration but stays calm. Opa's voice is warm and
unhurried. No music, no dramatic sting.

## Emotion

Warm curiosity meets a small obstacle. The puzzle piece almost fits — close enough to keep
trying, wrong enough to cause a pause. The feeling is light; frustration hasn't arrived yet.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No tantrum, no angry shouting, no thrown puzzle piece, no real candle or flame. Kiko's
frustration will grow in Shot 02. This shot is purely gentle — a problem that invites
patience, not a crisis.

## Negative Prompt

low quality, blurry, deformed, extra limbs, text, watermark, photorealistic, horror, scary,
dark lighting, sharp edges, hard surfaces, falling, dangerous height, crowd, competition,
tantrum, angry shouting, thrown puzzle piece, real candle, flame, fire, scolding, adult
correction tone, dramatic music, loud sound, fast movement, sudden camera motion, static
talking pose, characters frozen, background music, music, melody, song, soundtrack, redesigned
living room, changed rug colour, missing puzzle, broken puzzle, sharp puzzle edges, extra
characters, extra puzzle pieces

## QA Checklist

- [ ] Kiko + Opa identity preserved; voices established (Episode Colour Master).
- [ ] Kiko's Home living room identity preserved: soft toy rug, warm daylight, cozy shapes.
- [ ] The puzzle board is large, soft, round, and safe; no sharp edges.
- [ ] The puzzle piece is large, soft, round, and slightly tilted; problem reads mild.
- [ ] Opa is calm and present; no urgent or corrective tone.
- [ ] No on-screen text; calm but alive; no frozen pose.

#### BLD-EP11 — Shot 02 — It Won't Fit (Feeling)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP11 — Slow Breaths |
| Shot | 02 / 08 |
| Duration | 12 seconds |
| Location | Kiko's Home — Living Room / toy rug |
| Characters | Kiko, Opa |
| Time of Day | Warm Daytime |
| Spine step | FEELING |

## Purpose

Show Kiko's growing frustration — the puzzle piece still won't fit after a second attempt.
Kiko's body language shifts: shoulders tighten, brows furrow slightly. She pauses and says
"It won't fit." This creates the emotional gap that breathing will fill.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Kiko pushes the puzzle piece again — it still doesn't fit. The repeated
failure creates a small, readable frustration that any child recognises.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 01. The puzzle board is on the toy rug. The piece was already
slightly tilted; now Kiko tries once more and it still won't slot in. Opa remains calm and
nearby. Background locked from Shot 01.

## Environment Anchors

- Same Kiko's Home Living Room; soft toy rug remains the base.
- One large soft round puzzle board on the rug; piece still slightly misaligned.
- Opa nearby, watching calmly, not intervening yet.
- No new props, no new characters, no background movement.

## Background Object Lock

Identical to Shot 01. Background locked from first frame. Only Kiko, Opa, and the puzzle
pieces move. The toy rug, living room, and warm daylight remain stable.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Kiko's Home Living Room, warm daytime. Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown pigtails) sits on the soft
toy rug, trying to push a large soft round puzzle piece into the matching round puzzle board.
The piece still doesn't fit — she turns it, tries again, and it resists. Kiko's eyebrows
furrow slightly, her shoulders tighten. She pauses and says: "It won't fit." Opa (warm grey
sweater, soft features, gentle eyes) watches calmly nearby. Soft pastel colours, warm daylight,
rounded safe shapes, cozy living room, no other characters, {style} {camera} {lighting}

The Kiko's Home background is locked from the first frame; keep the soft toy rug, warm daylight
and cozy living room stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

Medium shot on Kiko and the puzzle board. Close-up on hands as the piece resists. Gentle
push-in on Kiko's face as frustration grows. Steady, calm movement — no fast cuts.

## Dialogue

```text
Kiko: It won't fit.
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-3 sec | Kiko pushes the puzzle piece into the board; it doesn't fit | Close-up on hands |
| 3-6 sec | She turns the piece, tries again; still doesn't slot in | Close-up hold |
| 6-9 sec | Kiko pauses: "It won't fit." Her brows furrow slightly | Medium on Kiko |
| 9-12 sec | Shoulders tighten; a small moment of frustration | Gentle push-in |

## Sound

Soft puzzle piece touches — gentle "pof pof" — but no satisfying click. Kiko's voice shows
mild frustration but stays calm. A quiet moment. No music, no dramatic sting.

## Emotion

The feeling grows — but remains controlled. Kiko doesn't throw the piece or shout; she simply
stops and says "It won't fit." This pause creates the opportunity for breathing and
calming down. Opa is still there, watching quietly.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No tantrum, no throwing piece, no crying, no angry shout, no slamming. Kiko's frustration is
a facial shift and body tension — not an explosion. The feeling is age-appropriate and
contained. Opa does not intervene yet.

## Negative Prompt

low quality, blurry, deformed, extra limbs, text, watermark, photorealistic, horror, scary,
dark lighting, sharp edges, hard surfaces, falling, dangerous height, crowd, competition,
tantrum, throwing piece, crying, angry shout, slamming, adult intervention, correction tone,
dramatic music, loud sound, fast movement, sudden camera motion, static talking pose,
characters frozen, background music, music, melody, song, soundtrack, redesigned living room,
changed rug colour, missing puzzle, broken puzzle, sharp puzzle edges, extra characters,
extra puzzle pieces, thrown piece, crying meltdown, shouting match

## QA Checklist

- [ ] Kiko's Home living room identity preserved: soft toy rug, warm daylight, cozy shapes.
- [ ] The puzzle piece still doesn't fit; frustration reads mild and age-appropriate.

- [ ] Opa remains calm and nearby; no intervention yet.
- [ ] No on-screen text; calm but alive; no frozen pose.

#### BLD-EP11 — Shot 03 — Let's Breathe (Support)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP11 — Slow Breaths |
| Shot | 03 / 08 |
| Duration | 12 seconds |
| Location | Kiko's Home — Living Room / toy rug |
| Characters | Kiko, Opa |
| Time of Day | Warm Daytime |
| Spine step | SUPPORT |

## Purpose

The emotional turning point: Opa approaches calmly, kneels to Kiko's eye level, and offers
the breathing invitation. This shot bridges the frustration to the calm-down technique.
Opa does not lecture — he joins Kiko.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Opa shifts closer to Kiko, lowers himself to eye level. His movement is
gentle and unhurried — a physical invitation, not a correction.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 02. Kiko is still sitting with the puzzle board, frustration
visible but contained. Opa has been nearby the whole time; now he moves closer. Background
locked from Shot 01.

## Environment Anchors

- Same Kiko's Home Living Room; soft toy rug remains the base.
- The puzzle board and piece remain on the rug; piece still misaligned.
- Opa now closer, kneeling at Kiko's eye level.
- No new props, no new characters, no background movement.

## Background Object Lock

Identical to Shots 01–02. Background locked from first frame. Only Kiko, Opa, and the puzzle
pieces move. The toy rug, living room, and warm daylight remain stable.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Kiko's Home Living Room, warm daytime. Opa (warm grey sweater, soft features, gentle eyes)
kneels down to Kiko's eye level on the soft toy rug. Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown pigtails)
sits with the puzzle board in front of her, frustration still visible. Opa speaks gently:
"Let's breathe." His voice is warm, not corrective. Kiko looks at Opa — her brows begin to
soften. Soft pastel colours, warm daylight, rounded safe shapes, cozy living room, no other
characters, {style} {camera} {lighting}

The Kiko's Home background is locked from the first frame; keep the soft toy rug, warm daylight
and cozy living room stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

Medium two-shot at child eye level. Slow, gentle push-in as Opa kneels closer. Camera holds
the connection between the two faces. No quick cuts, no dramatic angles.

## Dialogue

```text
Opa: Let's breathe.
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-3 sec | Opa shifts closer, kneels to Kiko's eye level | Medium, follows Opa |
| 3-6 sec | Opa speaks gently: "Let's breathe." | Close two-shot |
| 6-9 sec | Kiko looks at Opa; brows begin to soften | Close-up on Kiko |
| 9-12 sec | Both sit together, ready to breathe | Medium two-shot |

## Sound

Opa's voice is warm and inviting — "Let's breathe" is an invitation, not an instruction. A
quiet moment. No music, no dramatic underscore.

## Emotion

The support moment — Opa acknowledges Kiko's feeling ("you're having a big feeling, that's
okay") and offers to breathe together. Kiko's face begins to soften: someone is there with
her, not against her.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No scolding, no "calm down" command, no frustration from Opa, no hurry, no correction tone,
no "you shouldn't feel that way" message. Opa's approach is purely supportive — he joins
Kiko, not fixes her.

## Negative Prompt

low quality, blurry, deformed, extra limbs, text, watermark, photorealistic, horror, scary,
dark lighting, sharp edges, hard surfaces, falling, dangerous height, crowd, competition,
scolding, "calm down" command, frustration from Opa, hurry, correction tone, "you shouldn't
feel that way" message, dramatic music, loud sound, fast movement, sudden camera motion,
static talking pose, characters frozen, background music, music, melody, song, soundtrack,
redesigned living room, changed rug colour, extra characters, adult hand in frame, grabbing,
pushing, forcing calm

## QA Checklist

- [ ] Kiko's Home living room identity preserved: soft toy rug, warm daylight, cozy shapes.
- [ ] Opa kneels to Kiko's eye level; approach reads gentle and supportive.
- [ ] "Let's breathe" is an invitation, not a command.
- [ ] Kiko's brows begin to soften; the emotional shift starts here.
- [ ] No on-screen text; calm but alive; no frozen pose.

#### BLD-EP11 — Shot 04 — Breathing Together (Action)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP11 — Slow Breaths |
| Shot | 04 / 08 |
| Duration | 15 seconds |
| Location | Kiko's Home — Living Room / toy rug |
| Characters | Kiko, Opa |
| Time of Day | Warm Daytime |
| Spine step | ACTION |

## Purpose

Show the core breathing technique: Opa and Kiko breathe in together (like smelling a flower)
and breathe out together (like puffing a pompom). The metaphor is visual and intuitive — no
candle, no flame. The breathing is slow, rhythmic, and shared.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Opa and Kiko sit together on the toy rug, the puzzle board between them.
Opa begins the breathing — a slow, visible inhale through the nose. Kiko watches and begins
to follow.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 03. Both characters are now sitting together, ready to breathe.
The puzzle board remains on the rug between them. Background locked from Shot 01.

## Environment Anchors

- Same Kiko's Home Living Room; soft toy rug remains the base.
- The puzzle board and piece remain on the rug between them.
- Both characters sit facing each other at child eye level.
- No new props, no new characters, no background movement.

## Background Object Lock

Identical to Shots 01–03. Background locked from first frame. Only Kiko, Opa, and the puzzle
pieces move. The toy rug, living room, and warm daylight remain stable.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Kiko's Home Living Room, warm daytime. Opa (warm grey sweater, soft features, gentle eyes) and
Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown pigtails) sit facing each other on the soft toy rug, the round
puzzle board between them. Opa leads a slow breathing exercise: inhale through the nose like
smelling a flower, exhale slowly like puffing a pompom. Kiko follows — her chest rises and
falls with Opa's rhythm. Both faces soften. Soft pastel colours, warm daylight, rounded safe
shapes, cozy living room, no other characters, {style} {camera} {lighting}

The Kiko's Home background is locked from the first frame; keep the soft toy rug, warm daylight
and cozy living room stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

Close two-shot at child eye level. Camera holds steady as both characters breathe — the
rhythm is visible in their chests and faces. A very gentle push-in on Kiko's face as she
follows the breath. Slow, meditative movement.

## Dialogue

```text
Opa: Breathe in... and out.
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-3 sec | Opa begins slow inhale; Kiko watches and follows | Close two-shot |
| 3-7 sec | Both breathe in together — chest rises, eyes soften | Close hold |
| 7-11 sec | Both breathe out slowly — shoulders drop, faces relax | Close two-shot |
| 11-15 sec | Kiko's body visibly softens; a quiet moment of calm | Close-up on Kiko |

## Sound

Slow, rhythmic breathing — very soft, almost inaudible. Opa's voice guides gently: "Breathe
in... and out." A meditative, quiet moment. No music, no dramatic underscore.

## Emotion

The calming mechanism in action. Kiko's body responds to the shared breathing — shoulders
drop, face softens, tension releases. The flower-and-pompom metaphor makes the technique
intuitive and safe. No candle, no flame — just breath.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No candle, no flame, no fire, no blowing hard, no "angry breath," no scolding, no hurry,
no "faster," no visible breath vapor. The breathing is slow, gentle, and shared. Kiko follows
Opa's lead naturally — not forced.

## Negative Prompt

low quality, blurry, deformed, extra limbs, text, watermark, photorealistic, horror, scary,
dark lighting, sharp edges, hard surfaces, falling, dangerous height, crowd, competition,
candle, flame, fire, blowing hard, "angry breath," scolding, hurry, "faster," visible breath
vapor, dramatic music, loud sound, fast movement, sudden camera motion, static talking pose,
characters frozen, background music, music, melody, song, soundtrack, redesigned living room,
changed rug colour, extra characters, forced breathing, adult hand on chest, pushing down
shoulders, exaggerated exhale, visible wind

## QA Checklist

- [ ] Kiko + Opa identity preserved; expressions match emotional beat.
- [ ] Kiko's Home living room identity preserved: soft toy rug, warm daylight, cozy shapes.
- [ ] Breathing is slow and shared; chest rises and falls visibly.
- [ ] The flower-and-pompom metaphor is visual, not verbal.
- [ ] No candle, no flame, no blowing hard, no visible vapor.
- [ ] Kiko's body softens naturally; not forced or exaggerated.
- [ ] No on-screen text; calm but alive; no frozen pose.

#### BLD-EP11 — Shot 05 — Body Softens (Relief)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP11 — Slow Breaths |
| Shot | 05 / 08 |
| Duration | 12 seconds |
| Location | Kiko's Home — Living Room / toy rug |
| Characters | Kiko, Opa |
| Time of Day | Warm Daytime |
| Spine step | RELIEF |

## Purpose

The emotional payoff of breathing: Kiko's body visibly softens — shoulders drop, face relaxes,
brows unfurrow. She feels the calm and names it. The breathing worked, and Kiko can now see
the puzzle differently.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Kiko's shoulders slowly drop — a visible, physical release. Her face
softens, her breathing is even. The calm is earned, not imposed.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 04. The breathing exercise has just finished. Kiko's body is
responding to the shared breath. The puzzle board remains on the rug. Background locked from
Shot 01.

## Environment Anchors

- Same Kiko's Home Living Room; soft toy rug remains the base.
- The puzzle board and piece remain on the rug; piece still misaligned.
- Both characters still sitting together at child eye level.
- No new props, no new characters, no background movement.

## Background Object Lock

Identical to Shots 01–04. Background locked from first frame. Only Kiko, Opa, and the puzzle
pieces move. The toy rug, living room, and warm daylight remain stable.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Kiko's Home Living Room, warm daytime. Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown pigtails) sits on the soft
toy rug — her shoulders drop slowly, her face softens, her brows unfurrow. The breathing
worked. She looks at Opa (warm grey sweater, soft features, gentle eyes) and says: "I feel
better." Her voice is calm and genuine. The puzzle board sits between them on the rug. Soft
pastel colours, warm daylight, rounded safe shapes, cozy living room, no other characters,
{style} {camera} {lighting}
```

```text
Kiko: I feel better.
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|

| 6-9 sec | Kiko looks at Opa: "I feel better." | Medium two-shot |
| 9-12 sec | Opa smiles warmly; a quiet moment of shared calm | Close-up on Opa |

## Sound

A quiet moment — breathing has finished, only soft indoor ambience remains. Kiko's voice is
calm and genuine. No music, no triumphant sting.

## Emotion

Relief — the breathing worked. Kiko's body has calmed, her mind has opened. She can now
look at the puzzle with fresh eyes. The calm is real, not magical; it came from a shared,
gentle technique.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No sudden mood change, no dramatic transformation, no "magic fix," no adult praise, no "good
job breathing" reinforcement. The calm is natural and earned. Kiko's "I feel better" is a

## Negative Prompt

- [ ] Kiko's Home living room identity preserved: soft toy rug, warm daylight, cozy shapes.

- [ ] The piece is turned gently; the new angle is visible.
- [ ] "Maybe like this?" reads as curiosity and discovery.
- [ ] No on-screen text; calm but alive; no frozen pose.

## BLD-EP12 — "Gentle Hands" ⭐ (viewing #12)

- **Tema:** Kızınca vurmamak · **Mekan:** Kiko's Home / Playground · **Kadro:** Kiko, Arda
- **Repeated phrase:** "Hands are for helping, not hurting."
- **Spine:** (1) Oyuncak/oyun üstünde küçük anlaşmazlık. (2) Kiko öfkelenir, elleri gerilir (vurma dürtüsü).
  (3) Duraksar; Opa/Mimi "Breathe" hatırlatır (EP11 callback). (4) Kiko yavaş nefes alır, elini indirir,
  sözle anlatır. (5) Sorun sözle çözülür. (6) "Hands are for helping, not hurting." (7) Birlikte yardımlaşırlar.
  (8) Sıcak kapanış.
- **Safe-exposure / hassas:** Vurma ASLA gösterilmez — sadece *dürtü* (gerilen el) gösterilir ve durdurulur.
  Şiddet, ağlama krizi, korku yok. Çözüm nefes + söz.

### Scene Definition Starter

- **Kapsam kararı:** Tek ana set olarak **Kiko's Home — Living Room / toy rug** kullanılır.
  Playground alternatifi bırakılır; hassas davranış beat'i için evin güvenli ve düşük uyarımlı ortamı daha uygun.
- **Kadro kararı:** **Kiko + Arda**. Opa/Mimi fiziksel olarak eklenmez; EP11 nefes callback'i Kiko'nun
  kendi hatırlamasıyla gelir. Böylece sahne kalabalıklaşmaz.
- **Prop:** Bir yumuşak oyuncak araba veya büyük yuvarlak blok. Keskin tekerlek/metal/gerçek araç yok.
- **Safe-exposure:** Vurma, itme, temas, korkutma yok. Sadece Kiko'nun ellerinin kısa süre gerilmesi,
  sonra nefes alıp ellerini dizlerine indirmesi gösterilir.

| Shot | Spine | Scene amacı | Kısa tanım |
|---:|---|---|---|
| 01 | Problem | Oyuncak anlaşmazlığı | Kiko ve Arda aynı yumuşak oyuncak arabaya uzanır. |
| 02 | Feeling | Büyük duygu | Kiko'nun elleri gerilir; yüzü "big feeling" yaşar, temas yoktur. |
| 03 | Support | EP11 callback | Kiko durur ve fısıldar: "Breathe in, breathe out." |
| 04 | Action | Eller yumuşar | Kiko nefes alır, ellerini indirir ve sözle anlatır: "I want a turn." |
| 05 | Action | Sözle çözüm | Arda arabayı ortaya koyar; beraber kısa bir yol yaparlar. |
| 06 | Relief | Yardım eden eller | Kiko yolu düzeltir, Arda arabayı yavaşça sürer. |
| 07 | Lesson | Repeated phrase | Kiko: "Hands are for helping, not hurting." |
| 08 | Lesson | Sıcak kapanış | Kiko ve Arda arabayı birlikte park eder, elleriyle küçük dalga verir. |

#### BLD-EP12 — Shot 01 — One Toy Car (Problem)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP12 — Gentle Hands |
| Shot | 01 / 08 |
| Duration | 15 seconds |
| Location | Kiko's Home — Living Room / toy rug |
| Characters | Kiko, Arda |
| Time of Day | Warm Daytime |
| Spine step | PROBLEM |

## Purpose

Open with a simple, readable toy desire: Kiko and Arda both reach for the same soft toy car on
the play rug. The problem is small — not a fight, but a gentle sharing challenge between friends.

## Opening Hook

First 3–5 seconds: the soft rounded toy car sits in the middle of the play rug. Kiko and Arda
both notice it at the same time and reach for it — not aggressively, but with eager curiosity.

## Continuity

First story shot, after the shared Brave Little Days opening bumper. This shot establishes the
living room setting, the toy rug, and the two characters' relationship. Background: warm daytime
light, soft rug, rounded furniture, safe home environment.

- One soft rounded toy car in the centre of the rug; toy-like, no real vehicle styling.
- Warm daytime light through soft curtains; rounded furniture edges.
- No other characters, no background movement, no hard surfaces.

Only Kiko, Arda, and the soft toy car move.

Kiko, Arda, and the toy car. Stable settle only.


| 12-15 sec | Arda: "Can I try?" Kiko: "I want it too." | Medium hold |

## Sound

Soft home interior ambience: light curtain movement, warm room tone. The toy car makes a very
soft sound when touched. Natural ambience only. No music, no loud sounds, no competitive sound.

## Emotion

Warm curiosity and the beginning of a small sharing moment. No argument yet; the feeling is light.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No hitting, no pushing, no grabbing, no crying, no angry face, no punishment, no "bad hands"
shame. Both children's reaching is gentle and natural — not aggressive.
