#### BLD-EP12 — Shot 02 — Big Feeling (Feeling)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP12 — Gentle Hands |
| Shot | 02 / 08 |
| Duration | 12 seconds |
| Location | Kiko's Home — Living Room / toy rug |
| Characters | Kiko, Arda |
| Time of Day | Warm Daytime |
| Spine step | FEELING |

## Purpose

Show Kiko's big feeling — the impulse to hit. Her hands tense up briefly, her face shows the
internal conflict: she wants to act but stops herself. NO contact is made. This is the critical
moment where the impulse is shown and then stopped.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Kiko's hands tense up for a brief moment — the hitting impulse is visible
but does not become contact. Her face shows the "big feeling": brows furrow, jaw tightens,
chest rises with breath.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 01. Both children were reaching for the toy car. Now Kiko's
emotion intensifies. The background stays locked from Shot 01 — soft rug, rounded furniture,
warm daytime light.

## Environment Anchors

- Same Kiko's Home Living Room; soft rug on the floor.
- The soft rounded toy car sits between both characters.
- Kiko's hands are the focus — tense, then still.
- No new props, no new characters, no background movement.

## Background Object Lock

Identical to Shot 01. Background locked from first frame. Only Kiko, Arda, and the toy car
move. The rug, furniture, and warm light remain stable.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Kiko's Home Living Room, warm daytime. Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown pigtails) kneels on the
soft toy rug, her hands briefly tense — the hitting impulse is visible but does NOT become
contact. Her face shows big feeling: brows furrowed, jaw tightens, chest rises. Arda (green
shirt, brown curly hair) watches nearby, his expression shifting to mild concern. The soft
rounded toy car sits on the rug between them. NO contact is made. Soft pastel colours, warm
indoor light, rounded safe home shapes, no other characters, {style} {camera} {lighting}

The Living Room background is locked from the first frame; keep the soft rug, rounded furniture
and warm daytime light stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

Close-up on Kiko's hands and face, then slow pull-back to include Arda. Camera holds steady on
Kiko's internal moment — the impulse rising and being held. Gentle, unhurried.

## Dialogue

```text
Kiko: I want it!
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-3 sec | Kiko's hands tense up briefly — the impulse is visible | Close-up on hands |
| 3-6 sec | Kiko's face shows big feeling; brows furrow, jaw tightens | Close-up on Kiko |
| 6-9 sec | Kiko holds — hands still tense, but no contact made | Close hold |
| 9-12 sec | Kiko takes a deep breath; hands begin to soften | Medium on Kiko |

## Sound

A quiet moment — even breathing pauses. Kiko's "I want it!" is tense but controlled. Then
silence — the impulse is being held, not released.

## Emotion

Big feeling — the hitting impulse exists but is not acted on. Kiko's face shows internal
conflict: she wants to but doesn't. This is the critical window for breathing and calming down.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

NO hitting, NO pushing, NO contact, NO arm swinging, NO contact made, NO tears, NO shouting
match, NO scared face from Arda, NO punishment, NO adult hand stopping. The impulse is shown
only as tensed hands — it is stopped before becoming action.

## Negative Prompt

low quality, blurry, deformed, extra limbs, text, watermark, photorealistic, horror, scary,
dark lighting, sharp furniture, hard ground, falling, dangerous height, crowd, competition,
hitting, pushing, contact, arm swinging, contact made, tears, shouting match, scared face from
Arda, punishment, adult hand stopping, extra characters, fast movement, sudden camera motion,
static talking pose, characters frozen, background music, music, melody, song, soundtrack

## QA Checklist

- [ ] Kiko + Arda identity preserved; expressions match emotional beat.
- [ ] Kiko's Home Living Room identity preserved: soft rug, rounded furniture, warm light.
- [ ] The impulse is shown ONLY as tensed hands — NO contact, NO hitting, NO pushing.
- [ ] Kiko's big feeling reads genuine and age-appropriate; not exaggerated.
- [ ] Arda's mild concern reads natural; not fear or tears.
- [ ] No on-screen text; calm but alive; no frozen pose.

#### BLD-EP12 — Shot 03 — EP11 Callback: Breathe (Support)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP12 — Gentle Hands |
| Shot | 03 / 08 |

| Location | Kiko's Home — Living Room / toy rug |

The emotional turning point: Kiko pauses and remembers the breathing technique from EP11.

#### BLD-EP12 — Shot 04 — Hands Soften (Action)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP12 — Gentle Hands |
| Shot | 04 / 08 |
| Duration | 12 seconds |
| Location | Kiko's Home — Living Room / toy rug |
| Characters | Kiko, Arda |
| Time of Day | Warm Daytime |
| Spine step | ACTION |

## Purpose

Show the physical transformation: after breathing, Kiko's hands soften — tension drops, fingers
open, hands lower to her lap. She can now speak calmly. This is the moment where "vurma
yerine konuşma" (speaking instead of hitting) becomes visible.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Close-up on Kiko's hands — the tension visibly releases. Fingers uncurl,
palms open, hands settle onto her knees. The transformation is physical and immediate.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 03. Kiko has just whispered "Breathe in, breathe out" and taken
a deep breath. Now her body responds. Background remains locked.

## Environment Anchors

- Same Kiko's Home Living Room; soft rug on the floor.
- The soft rounded toy car sits between both characters.
- Kiko's hands move from tense to soft — the visual core of this shot.
- No new props, no new characters, no background movement.

## Background Object Lock

Identical to Shots 01–03. Background locked from first frame. Only Kiko, Arda, and the toy
car move. The rug, furniture, and warm light remain stable.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Kiko's Home Living Room, warm daytime. Close-up on Kiko's (coral pink shirt, brown pigtails)
hands as they visibly soften — tension drops, fingers uncurl, palms open, hands settle onto
her knees. Her face relaxes. She looks at Arda (green shirt, brown curly hair) and speaks
calmly: "I want a turn." The soft rounded toy car sits on the rug between them. Soft pastel
colours, warm indoor light, rounded safe home shapes, no other characters, {style} {camera}
{lighting}

The Living Room background is locked from the first frame; keep the soft rug, rounded furniture
and warm daytime light stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

Close-up on Kiko's hands as they soften, then slow tilt up to her face. Camera follows the
physical transformation. A soft pull-back to include Arda as Kiko speaks. Steady and calm.

## Dialogue

```text
Kiko: I want a turn.
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-3 sec | Kiko's hands soften — tension drops, fingers open | Close-up on hands |
| 3-6 sec | Hands settle on her knees; face relaxes | Tilt up to face |
| 6-9 sec | Kiko looks at Arda: "I want a turn." | Medium two-shot |
| 9-12 sec | Arda listens; face shows a ready response | Close-up on Arda |

## Sound

A quiet moment — the breathing is done, the hands are soft. Kiko's voice is calm and clear:
"I want a turn." No tension, no demand — just words.

## Emotion

Speaking instead of hitting — Kiko stopped the impulse, breathed, and can now express what she
wants with words. This is the most critical moment of EP12: words instead of hands.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No begging, no whining, no demanding tone, no finger pointing, no "give it to me," no
aggressive body language. Kiko's voice is calm, clear, and respectful.

## Negative Prompt

low quality, blurry, deformed, extra limbs, text, watermark, photorealistic, horror, scary,
dark lighting, sharp furniture, hard ground, falling, dangerous height, crowd, competition,
hitting, pushing, contact, begging, whining, demanding tone, finger pointing, aggressive body
language, extra characters, fast movement, sudden camera motion, static talking pose, characters
frozen, background music, music, melody, song, soundtrack

## QA Checklist

#### BLD-EP12 — Shot 07 — Hands Are for Helping (Lesson)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP12 — Gentle Hands |
| Shot | 07 / 08 |
| Duration | 12 seconds |
| Location | Kiko's Home — Living Room / toy rug |
| Characters | Kiko, Arda |
| Time of Day | Warm Daytime |
| Spine step | LESSON |

## Purpose

The repeated phrase moment: Kiko parks the car with Arda, looks at her hands, then delivers
"Hands are for helping, not hurting." This is a shared discovery, not a lecture.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Kiko and Arda park the toy car together on the rug. Kiko looks down at
her own hands — a quiet moment of recognition before she speaks.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 06. The car has been driven along the soft road. Now both
children park it together. Kiko's hands, which were tense in Shot 02, are now soft and calm.

## Environment Anchors

- Same Kiko's Home Living Room; soft rug on the floor.
- The soft rounded toy car is parked between both characters.
- Kiko looks at her hands, then at Arda.
- No new props, no new characters, no background movement.

## Background Object Lock

Identical to Shots 01–06. Background locked from first frame. Only Kiko, Arda, and the toy
car move. The rug, furniture, and warm light remain stable.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Kiko's Home Living Room, warm daytime. Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown pigtails) and Arda (green
shirt, brown curly hair) park the soft rounded toy car together on the toy rug. Kiko looks down
at her own hands — a quiet moment of recognition. Then she looks at Arda and says: "Hands are
for helping, not hurting." Her voice is warm and sincere. Arda smiles. Soft pastel colours, warm
indoor light, rounded safe home shapes, no other characters, {style} {camera} {lighting}

The Living Room background is locked from the first frame; keep the soft rug, rounded furniture
and warm daytime light stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

Medium two-shot as they park the car, then close-up on Kiko's hands, then back to her face
as she speaks. A gentle, intimate framing that follows Kiko's internal realization.

## Dialogue

```text
Kiko: Hands are for helping, not hurting.
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-3 sec | Kiko and Arda park the car together | Medium two-shot |
| 3-6 sec | Kiko looks at her hands — quiet recognition | Close-up on hands |
| 6-9 sec | Kiko: "Hands are for helping, not hurting." | Close-up on Kiko |
| 9-12 sec | Arda smiles; both feel comfortable | Two-shot hold |

## Sound

Kiko's voice is warm and sincere — she's not teaching, she's sharing something she discovered.
A gentle, heartfelt tone. No dramatic music, no triumphant sting.

## Emotion

The repeated phrase — Kiko shares a truth that came from her own experience. This is not a
rule being taught; it's a discovery being shared: our hands are for helping, not hurting.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No preachy tone, no moralizing, no adult voice-off, no lecture face, no finger wagging, no
"remember this" teaching moment. Kiko's delivery is natural and personal.

## Negative Prompt

dark lighting, sharp furniture, hard ground, falling, dangerous height, crowd, competition,

- [ ] Kiko's Home Living Room identity preserved: soft rug, rounded furniture, warm light.

## BLD-EP13 — "A Little Tumble" (viewing #13)

- **Tema:** Kaza sonrası yardım isteme · **Mekan:** Playground / Kiko's Home garden · **Kadro:** Kiko, Mimi (+ adult)
- **Repeated phrase:** "It's okay — I can ask for help."
- **Spine:** (1) Kiko koşarken hafifçe takılıp düşer (küçük). (2) Dizi "ouch", ürker. (3) Panik yerine
  bir büyüğe seslenir. (4) Büyük nazikçe bakar, küçük bir yara bandı. (5) Kiko rahatlar. (6) "It's okay —
  I can ask for help." (7) Tekrar oynamaya döner. (8) Sıcak kapanış.
- **Safe-exposure:** Düşme çok hafif; KAN/ciddi yara YOK. Sadece küçük "ouch" + yara bandı. Ağlama krizi yok.

### Scene Definition Starter

- **Kapsam kararı:** Tek ana set olarak **Benny's Playground — Rest Corner / soft grass edge** kullanılır.
  Kiko's Home garden alternatif kalır; playground zaten yumuşak zemin ve yardım isteme temasını destekler.
- **Kadro kararı:** **Kiko, Mimi, Opa**. Opa en baştan Rest Corner'da görünür; aniden belirmez.
- **Canon uyarlaması:** Draft'taki "koşarken" beat'i çocuk güvenliği nedeniyle **yavaş yürürken küçük
  tökezleme / soft sit-down** olarak yumuşatılır. Koşma, sert düşme, çarpma sesi yok.
- **Safe-exposure:** Kan, yara, morluk yok. Bandage varsa "soft star bandage sticker" olarak okunur;
  gerçek yara kapatma görüntüsü değil, rahatlatıcı sembol.

| Shot | Spine | Scene amacı | Kısa tanım |
|---:|---|---|---|
| 01 | Problem | Yumuşak oyun alanı | Kiko ve Mimi Rest Corner yakınında yavaşça yürür; Opa bankta görünür. |
| 02 | Problem/Feeling | Küçük tökezleme | Kiko yumuşak topa/çim kıvrımına takılıp çimene oturur: "Ouch." |
| 03 | Support | Yardım isteme | Kiko paniğe kapılmaz; Opa'ya döner: "Help, please." |
| 04 | Action | Nazik kontrol | Opa yaklaşır, diz hizasında çöker: "I'm here." |
| 05 | Action | Rahatlatıcı bakım | Opa soft star bandage sticker verir; Mimi Kiko'nun yanında kalır. |
| 06 | Relief | Rahatlama | Kiko nefes verir: "I'm okay." |
| 07 | Relief | Oyuna dönüş | Kiko yavaşça ayağa kalkar; Mimi ile küçük bir adım atar. |
| 08 | Lesson | Sıcak kapanış | "It's okay — I can ask for help." Kapanışta üçü sıcak gülümser. |

#### BLD-EP13 — Shot 01 — Walking Near the Rest Corner (Problem)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |

#### BLD-EP13 — Shot 02 — A Little Tumble (Problem/Feeling)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP13 — A Little Tumble |
| Shot | 02 / 08 |
| Duration | 12 seconds |

grass — a "soft sit-down," not a hard fall. The "ouch" is mild surprise, not pain. No blood,
no wound, no drama.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Kiko walks slowly on the soft grass; her foot catches on a soft surface


## Emotion

A small tumble — but controlled. Kiko doesn't panic; she just stops and processes what

## Safe-Exposure Notes

- [ ] No blood, no wound, no crying, no screaming.
- [ ] No on-screen text; calm but alive; no frozen pose.

#### BLD-EP13 — Shot 03 — Asking for Help (Support)

#### BLD-EP13 — Shot 05 — Comfort Care (Action)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP13 — A Little Tumble |
| Shot | 05 / 08 |
| Duration | 12 seconds |

| Time of Day | Warm Morning |
| Spine step | ACTION |

## Purpose

Opa gives Kiko a soft star bandage sticker — not a real bandage for a real wound, but a
comforting symbol. The sticker represents care and attention, not medical treatment. Kiko's
response is "I'm being cared for," not "I'm healed."

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Opa reaches into his pocket and pulls out a soft star-shaped sticker.

curiosity.

sticker from his pocket. Background remains locked from Shot 01.

- Soft grass, rounded playground equipment in background.
- One soft playground ball at ground level near the bench.
- Opa kneeling beside Kiko; Mimi nearby.
- Warm morning light, soft pastel colours, no extra characters.

move. The low rest bench, soft grass, rounded equipment, and soft playground ball remain stable.

## Visual Prompt


#### BLD-EP13 — Shot 08 — Warm Closing (Lesson)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP13 — A Little Tumble |

| Duration | 12 seconds |

## Purpose

The warm closing shot: all three characters stand together, smiling. Kiko delivers the
repeated phrase one final time — "It's okay — I can ask for help." This is not a lecture
but a shared discovery. The lesson is sealed with warmth and friendship.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Kiko, Mimi, and Opa stand together near the Rest Corner. All three
smile warmly. The star sticker is visible on Kiko's knee. The scene feels complete and
warm.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 07. Kiko and Mimi have returned to play; now all three
characters come together for the closing moment. Background remains locked from Shot 01.

- Same Benny's Playground Rest Corner; low rest bench visible.
- Soft grass, rounded playground equipment in background.
- One soft playground ball at ground level near the bench.
- Star sticker on Kiko's knee.
- All three characters standing together, facing camera.

## Background Object Lock

Identical to Shots 01–07. Background locked from first frame. Only Kiko, Mimi, and Opa
move. The low rest bench, soft grass, rounded equipment, soft playground ball, and star
sticker on Kiko's knee remain stable.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Benny's Playground Rest Corner, warm morning. Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown pigtails), Mimi
(lavender shirt, blonde pigtails), and Opa (warm brown vest, grey hair, glasses) stand
```


## Shot Breakdown

| 9-12 sec | All three give a small gentle wave; scene holds | Wide hold, gentle fade |

## Sound

Warm, intimate voice tones — Kiko's phrase is calm and sincere. Soft laughter from all
three, very gentle, almost inaudible. Soft playground ambience fades gently to end. No

## Emotion

Warm closing — "It's okay — I can ask for help." This is not a rule but a discovery:
asking for help is not weakness, it's strength. Kiko experienced it and learned it. The
feeling is one of gentle accomplishment and warm friendship.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No moralizing, no lecture, no adult voice-over, no on-screen text, no dramatic music, no
lesson-on-screen, no exaggerated wave, no preachy tone. The repeated phrase is delivered
as a shared discovery, not a rule being taught. The wave is friendly and inclusive.

soundtrack, drama, urgency, forced lesson

- [ ] Benny's Playground Rest Corner identity preserved: low bench, soft grass, rounded equipment.

- [ ] "It's okay — I can ask for help" delivered as shared discovery; not lecture.
- [ ] The wave is gentle and friendly; not exaggerated.
- [ ] No on-screen text; calm but alive; no frozen pose.
- [ ] The closing feels warm and complete — no loose ends.

---

## BLD-EP14 — "If I Get Lost" ⭐🆕 (viewing #14)

- **Tema:** Kaybolunca ne yapmalı · **Mekan:** Central Square (kalabalık gün) · **Kadro:** Kiko + güvenli helper (Opa/Remi/Nella)
- **Repeated phrase:** "Stay calm, find a helper."
- **Spine:** (1) Kalabalık meydanda Kiko büyüğünü göremez. (2) Bir an endişelenir. (3) Hatırlar: dur, sakin ol.
  (4) Tanıdık güvenli bir helper'a (Nella/Remi/Opa) gidip yardım ister. (5) Helper sakinleştirir, birlikte beklerler.
  (6) Büyüğüyle buluşur. (7) Rahatlama. (8) "Stay calm, find a helper."
- **🆕 Yeni canon / hassas:** "Kalabalık gün" (birkaç arka plan karakteri, canon max'a uygun). Yabancı-tehdidi
  YOK; güvenli helper tanıdık bir Pompom Hills karakteridir. Panik/ağlama krizi yok. → Onay gerekir.

### Scene Definition Starter — Pending Canon Approval

- **Kapsam kararı (öneri):** Tek ana set olarak **Central Square — Big Pompom Tree / Care Corner edge**
  kullanılır. "Kalabalık gün" yalnızca **2 sessiz arka plan karakteri** + ana aksiyon olarak tanımlanır;
  büyük kalabalık yok.
- **Helper kararı (öneri):** Güvenli helper olarak **Remi** kullanılır; Remi zaten Central Square Care Corner
  set-piece'iyle kanonda vardır. Opa, Kiko'nun kısa süre göremediği güvenli büyüktür ve bölüm sonunda yeniden
  görünür.
- **Canon notu:** Bu starter canon dosyalarını değiştirmez. Üretimden önce "light crowd day" ve Remi'nin
  genel safe-helper kullanımı onaylanmalıdır.
- **Safe-exposure:** Kiko gerçekten kaybolmuş gibi korkutulmaz; yalnızca Opa'yı bir an göremez. Yabancı tehdidi,
  panik, ağlama krizi, yalnız bırakılma ve karanlık yok.

| Shot | Spine | Scene amacı | Kısa tanım |
|---:|---|---|---|
| 01 | Problem | Meydan biraz daha hareketli | Kiko ve Opa Big Pompom Tree yakınında yürür; iki sessiz arka plan figürü uzak kenarda selamlaşır. |
| 02 | Feeling | Opa'yı görememe | Kiko bir an durur; Opa tree trunk / background hareketi yüzünden kadraj dışında kalmıştır. |
| 03 | Support | Hatırlama | Kiko ellerini göğsünde tutar, sakin nefes alır: "Stay calm." |
| 04 | Action | Tanıdık helper'a gitme | Kiko Care Corner kenarında bekleyen Remi'ye yavaşça yaklaşır. |
| 05 | Support | Birlikte bekleme | Remi çömelir, sıcak sesle "I can help" der; Kiko yanında kalır. |
| 06 | Relief | Opa yeniden görünür | Opa Big Pompom Tree yanından görünür ve sakin şekilde yaklaşır. |
| 07 | Relief | Güvenli buluşma | Kiko rahatlar; Remi ve Opa küçük bir güven gülümsemesi paylaşır. |
| 08 | Lesson | Sıcak kapanış | Kiko, Opa ve Remi: "Stay calm, find a helper." |

#### BLD-EP14 — Shot 01 — A Busy-But-Gentle Square (Problem)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP14 — If I Get Lost |
| Shot | 01 / 08 |
| Duration | 15 seconds |
| Location | Central Square — Big Pompom Tree / Care Corner edge |
| Characters | Kiko, Opa |
| Time of Day | Warm Morning |
| Spine step | PROBLEM |

## Purpose

Open the episode in a slightly livelier Central Square — not a crowd, but a gentle buzz of
activity. Kiko and Opa walk together near the Big Pompom Tree. Two silent background figures
are visible at the far edge, adding life without chaos. This shot establishes the "busy day"
feeling that sets up the separation in Shot 02.

## Opening Hook

First 3–5 seconds: Central Square is warm and bright, a touch more alive than usual. Two
silent background figures are visible at the far edge, waving gently at each other. Kiko
and Opa walk together near the Big Pompom Tree.

## Continuity

First story shot, after the shared Brave Little Days opening bumper. This shot establishes
the slightly busier Central Square and the two main characters walking together. Background:
Big Pompom Tree centred, soft grass, warm morning light, Care Corner awning at soft edge.

## Environment Anchors

- Central Square — Big Pompom Tree (`CS-TREE-01`) centred as the primary landmark.
- Care Corner visible only as a soft edge set-piece (muted awning) — not the focus.
- Two silent background figures at the far edge; they wave gently at each other.
- Soft green grass, rounded safe shapes, warm morning light.
- No more than 2 background figures; no crowd.

## Background Object Lock

Background locked from first frame. Keep `CS-TREE-01` centred, soft grass, rounded equipment,
and Care Corner awning stable. Only Kiko, Opa, and the two background figures move.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Central Square near Big Pompom Tree, warm morning. Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown pigtails) and
Opa (cream vest, round glasses, grey hair) walk together on soft green grass. The Big Pompom Tree
is centred in the background, its soft rounded canopy visible. Two silent background figures stand
at the far edge of the square, waving gently at each other — small, distant, not intrusive. Care
Corner awning is a soft muted shape at the edge. Soft pastel colours, warm light, rounded safe
shapes, gentle ambient life, {style} {camera} {lighting}

The Central Square background is locked from the first frame; keep Big Pompom Tree, soft grass,
rounded equipment and Care Corner awning stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

32mm wide at child eye level establishing Central Square and Big Pompom Tree; slow settle to
medium on Kiko and Opa walking together. The two background figures are visible at the edge but
do not dominate. Stable settle only.

## Dialogue

```text
Kiko: So many friends.

Opa: Stay close, Kiko.
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-4 sec | Central Square visible; two background figures wave at the edge | Wide |
| 4-8 sec | Kiko and Opa walk together near Big Pompom Tree | Settle |
| 8-12 sec | Kiko looks around: "So many friends." | Medium on Kiko |
| 12-15 sec | Opa gently: "Stay close, Kiko." They continue walking | Medium hold |

## Sound

Soft Central Square ambience: birds, light breeze, a very gentle murmur of distant activity.
Natural ambience only. No music, no loud sounds, no crowd noise.

## Emotion

Warm, gentle curiosity — Kiko notices the slightly livelier square with interest, not anxiety.
Opa's reminder is calm and loving, not anxious. The feeling is safe and open.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No real crowd, no stranger danger, no panic, no shouting, no running. The two background
figures are silent and distant — they add life without creating overwhelm. Kiko feels safe
with Opa beside her.

## Negative Prompt

- [ ] Care Corner visible only as soft awning edge; not the focus.
- [ ] The square feels gently lively but not overwhelming.
- [ ] No on-screen text; calm but alive; no frozen pose.

#### BLD-EP14 — Shot 02 — Where's Opa? (Feeling)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP14 — If I Get Lost |
| Shot | 02 / 08 |
| Duration | 12 seconds |
| Location | Central Square — Big Pompom Tree / Care Corner edge |
| Characters | Kiko |
| Time of Day | Warm Morning |
| Spine step | FEELING |

## Purpose

Show the moment Kiko realizes she can't see Opa — a brief, gentle worry without panic. Opa is
simply out of frame behind the tree trunk or background movement. Kiko stops, looks, and says
"Opa?" — a question, not a cry for help. The feeling is "someone's missing," not "I'm lost."

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Kiko stops walking. She looks around — Opa was just beside her but is now
out of frame. Her expression shifts from relaxed to mildly curious. No panic, no fear.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 01. Kiko and Opa were walking together; now Opa is temporarily
out of view. The background remains locked — Big Pompom Tree centred, soft grass, warm light.

#### BLD-EP14 — Shot 03 — Stay Calm (Support)

```text
{style} {camera} {lighting}

The Central Square background is locked from the first frame; keep Big Pompom Tree, soft grass,
```

Reunion — Opa is here, everything is okay. Kiko's relief is natural and warm. Opa's "There

#### BLD-EP14 — Shot 08 — Warm Closing (Lesson)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|

The warm closing shot: Kiko, Opa, and Remi stand together. Kiko delivers the repeated phrase

experience. The three share a gentle wave to the camera, sealing the lesson with warmth.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: The three stand together on soft grass near the Big Pompom Tree. Kiko is
beside Opa, safe and relaxed. All three face the camera with warm, gentle smiles.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 07. The gratitude exchange is complete. Now the three share the
final moment together. Background remains locked — Big Pompom Tree centred, soft grass, warm light.

## Environment Anchors

- Care Corner visible as soft edge set-piece.
- Two silent background figures remain at the far edge.
- Kiko, Opa, and Remi stand together, facing the camera.
- No new props, no new characters, no background movement.

```text

```

| 9-12 sec | All three give a small gentle wave; scene holds for fade | Gentle pull-back |

## Sound

Warm, natural voices — Kiko's delivery is sincere and personal, not preachy. Soft laughter
from the group — very gentle, almost inaudible. Natural ambience carries to the end. No music,
no outro sting.

## Emotion

Warm closure — "Stay calm, find a helper" is delivered as a shared discovery, not a rule.
Kiko lived this experience and now shares what she learned. The feeling is gentle
accomplishment and community warmth.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No moralizing, no lecture, no adult voice-over. The repeated phrase is Kiko's own — spoken

## BLD-EP15 — "Stop, Look, Cross" ⭐🆕 (viewing #15)

- **Tema:** Yolda güvenli yürümek · **Mekan:** 🆕 **Pompom Crossing** (yeni set-piece) · **Kadro:** Kiko, Opa
- **Repeated phrase:** "Stop, look, hold a hand."
- **Spine:** (1) Kiko & Opa soft crossing practice path'e gelir; Kiko hevesle ileri adım atmak ister.
  (2) Opa "Wait — stop." (3) El/kanat ucu tutma. (4) Renk sinyaline bakma (soft coral → soft green).
  (5) Sağa-sola bakarlar. (6) Birlikte, el ele/kanat ucu tutarak geçerler. (7) "We did it safely!"
  (8) "Stop, look, hold a hand."
- **🆕 Yeni canon:** Pompom Crossing gerçek cadde değil; çimen üstünde soft practice path + iki yuvarlak renk
  sinyali olan yumuşak bir set-piece olmalıdır. Yol/asfalt/araç/trafik YOK. → Set onayı gerekir.

### Scene Definition Starter — Pending New Set Approval

- **Kapsam kararı (güvenlik uyarlaması):** **Pompom Crossing** gerçek cadde değildir. Önerilen set, Central
  Square yakınında veya ayrı küçük bir alanda duran **soft crossing practice path** olarak ele alınır:
  çimen üstünde geniş, yuvarlak stepping-stone bandı + iki yuvarlak renk sinyali. Asfalt, şehir yolu, araç,
  motor sesi ve modern trafik mobilyası yok.
- **Kadro kararı:** **Kiko + Opa**. Opa rehberdir; Kiko'nun elini/kanat ucunu tutarak modeli gösterir.
- **Canon notu:** Yeni set-piece üretimden önce canonlanmalıdır. Bu starter yalnızca çocuk güvenliğine uyarlanmış
  öneridir; canon dosyası güncellenmez.
- **Safe-exposure:** "Koşmak ister" beat'i **eager step** olarak yumuşatılır. Kiko koşmaz, yola fırlamaz,
  araç trafiği görmez. Öğrenme modeli: dur, bak, el tut.

| Shot | Spine | Scene amacı | Kısa tanım |
|---:|---|---|---|
| 01 | Problem | Crossing path'e varış | Kiko ve Opa soft stepping-stone crossing path'in başına gelir; Kiko ileri adım atmak ister. |
| 02 | Feeling | Bekleme zor gelir | Opa yumuşakça "Stop first" der; Kiko durur. |
| 03 | Support | El/kanat tutma | Opa kanat ucunu uzatır, Kiko tutar. |
| 04 | Action | Renk sinyaline bakma | Yumuşak coral stop disc'ten soft green go disc'e geçiş olur; text yok. |
| 05 | Action | Sağa sola bakma | İkisi beraber yavaşça iki yana bakar; dünya sakin ve boştur. |
| 06 | Action | Birlikte geçme | Kiko ve Opa el ele/kanat ucu tutarak stepping-stone bandı geçer. |
| 07 | Relief | Güvenli varış | Kiko karşı tarafta gülümser: "We did it safely." |
| 08 | Lesson | Sıcak kapanış | "Stop, look, hold a hand." tekrar edilir. |

#### BLD-EP15 — Shot 01 — The Soft Crossing Path (Problem)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP15 — Stop, Look, Cross |
| Shot | 01 / 08 |
| Duration | 15 seconds |
| Location | Pompom Crossing — proposed soft crossing practice path |
| Characters | Kiko, Opa |
| Time of Day | Warm Morning |
| Spine step | PROBLEM |

## Purpose

Open with a readable arrival at the soft crossing practice path. Kiko and Opa arrive at the
beginning of the Pompom Crossing — a wide soft stepping-stone band on grass with two round
colour discs. Kiko wants to step forward eagerly; this sets up the learning need.

## Opening Hook

First 3–5 seconds: The wide soft stepping-stone band stretches across green grass. Two round
colour discs sit at the near end — one coral, one green. Kiko and Opa stand at the start.
Kiko leans forward, one foot ready to step.

## Continuity

First story shot, after the shared Brave Little Days opening bumper. This shot's approved
first-frame still = **Episode Colour Master**. Maintain Kiko + Opa identity, Pompom Crossing
world identity, warm morning light. Do not redesign the crossing path or add road elements.

## Environment Anchors

- Pompom Crossing practice path: wide soft stepping-stone band on soft green grass.
- Two round colour discs: soft coral (stop) and soft green (go), visible at the near end.
- No road, no asphalt, no cars, no traffic, no urban infrastructure.
- Warm morning light, soft green grass, rounded safe shapes. No extra characters.

## Background Object Lock

Background locked from first frame. Keep the stepping-stone band, colour discs, soft grass,
and rounded surroundings stable. Only Kiko, Opa, and the colour discs move.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Pompom Crossing soft practice path, warm morning. A wide soft stepping-stone band stretches
across soft green grass — round, flat, pastel-coloured stones. Two round colour discs sit at
the near end: one soft coral (stop), one soft green (go). No road, no asphalt, no cars, no
traffic. Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown pigtails) stands at the start, one foot ready to step
forward eagerly. Opa (warm green, soft bird-like elder) stands beside her, calm and gentle.
Soft pastel colours, warm light, rounded safe shapes, no other characters, {style} {camera}
{lighting}

The Pompom Crossing background is locked from the first frame; keep the stepping-stone band,
colour discs, soft grass and rounded surroundings stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

32mm wide at child eye level establishing the Pompom Crossing practice path and colour discs;
slow settle to medium on Kiko, Opa, and the stepping-stone band. Stable settle only.

## Dialogue

```text
Kiko: I can go!

Opa: Stop first.
```

|---|---|---|
| 0-4 sec | Pompom Crossing practice path visible; stepping-stone band and colour discs | Wide |
| 4-8 sec | Kiko and Opa arrive at the start; Kiko leans forward eagerly | Settle |
| 8-12 sec | Kiko: "I can go!" — one foot ready to step | Medium |
| 12-15 sec | Opa calmly: "Stop first." | Medium hold |

## Sound

Soft playground ambience: birds, light breeze. Natural ambience only. No music, no traffic
sound, no engine noise, no urban ambience.

## Emotion

Warm curiosity and eagerness. Kiko wants to go — the path looks inviting and safe. Opa's
gentle "Stop first" introduces the first learning beat without tension.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No road, no cars, no traffic, no danger. This is a soft practice path on grass — a safe
learning environment. Kiko's eagerness is natural and age-appropriate; Opa's guidance is
calm and warm, not restrictive.

## Negative Prompt

#### BLD-EP15 — Shot 02 — Wait First (Feeling)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP15 — Stop, Look, Cross |

Show that waiting is hard for Kiko — she wants to go, but Opa's gentle "Stop first" makes

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Kiko takes a small eager step forward; Opa gently raises his hand. The

## Sound

Soft playground ambience continues: birds, light breeze. Opa's voice is calm and warm —
"Stop first" is a reminder, not a command. Kiko's "Okay" is warm and accepting.

## Emotion

The tension between eagerness and patience. Kiko wants to go — the path looks fun — but

#### BLD-EP15 — Shot 03 — Hold My Hand (Support)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP15 — Stop, Look, Cross |
| Shot | 03 / 08 |
| Duration | 12 seconds |
| Location | Pompom Crossing — proposed soft crossing practice path |
| Characters | Kiko, Opa |
| Time of Day | Warm Morning |
| Spine step | SUPPORT |

## Purpose

The trust-building moment: Opa offers his hand/wing-tip, and Kiko takes it. Holding hands
means they will cross together — this is the physical commitment to safety.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Opa extends his soft wing-tip toward Kiko. The gesture is warm and
inviting — a silent offer of togetherness.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 02. Kiko has just said "Okay" to waiting. Now Opa offers
his hand for the crossing. Background remains locked.

## Environment Anchors

- Same Pompom Crossing practice path; stepping-stone band and colour discs visible.
- Opa's wing-tip extended toward Kiko; Kiko's hand reaching for it.
- No road, no asphalt, no cars, no traffic.
- No new props, no new characters, no background movement.

## Background Object Lock

Identical to Shots 01–02. Background locked from first frame. Only Kiko and Opa move.
The stepping-stone band, colour discs, and soft grass remain stable.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Pompom Crossing soft practice path, warm morning. Opa (warm green, soft bird-like elder)
extends his soft wing-tip toward Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown pigtails). Kiko reaches out
and takes Opa's wing-tip with her small hand. Their hands/wing-tips connect gently — a
moment of trust. Both characters stand at the start of the soft stepping-stone band. Two
round colour discs visible. Soft pastel colours, warm light, rounded safe shapes, no other
characters, {style} {camera} {lighting}

The Pompom Crossing background is locked from the first frame; keep the stepping-stone band,
colour discs, soft grass and rounded surroundings stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

hands at the path start.

## Dialogue

```text
Opa: Hold my hand.
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-3 sec | Opa extends his wing-tip toward Kiko | Close-up on wing-tip |
| 3-6 sec | Kiko reaches out; their hands/wing-tips connect | Close-up, hands connect |
| 6-9 sec | Camera pulls back to medium two-shot; both hold hands | Pull-back to medium |
| 9-12 sec | They stand together at the path start, ready | Medium hold |

## Sound

A soft, quiet moment — the gentle touch of hands connecting. Opa's voice is warm and
inviting. Soft playground ambience continues in the background.

## Emotion

Trust and togetherness. Kiko holds Opa's hand — she knows they will cross together. The
physical connection makes her feel safe and supported. This is the foundation for everything
that follows.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No hand grab from Opa, no forced grip, no "you must hold" demand, no fear-based compliance,
no pulling. Opa offers; Kiko chooses to take. The connection is mutual and warm.

## Negative Prompt

- [ ] Opa offers gently; Kiko chooses to take — no grabbing, no pulling.

#### BLD-EP15 — Shot 04 — Watch the Colour (Action)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP15 — Stop, Look, Cross |
| Shot | 04 / 08 |
| Duration | 12 seconds |
| Location | Pompom Crossing — proposed soft crossing practice path |
| Characters | Kiko, Opa |
| Time of Day | Warm Morning |
| Spine step | ACTION |

## Purpose

Teach the colour signal: the soft coral disc (stop) transitions to soft green (go). Kiko and
Opa watch the colour change together — no text, only colour. This teaches "wait for green."

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: The soft coral stop disc glows gently. Kiko and Opa stand together,
holding hands, watching the disc. The coral colour is warm and clear.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 03. Kiko and Opa are now holding hands at the path start.
They watch the colour disc together. Background remains locked.

## Environment Anchors

- Same Pompom Crossing practice path; stepping-stone band visible.
- Two round colour discs: soft coral (currently lit) and soft green (off).
- Kiko and Opa holding hands, facing the discs.
- No road, no asphalt, no cars, no traffic.
- No new props, no new characters, no background movement.

## Background Object Lock

Identical to Shots 01–03. Background locked from first frame. Only Kiko, Opa, and the
colour discs' glow change move. The stepping-stone band and soft grass remain stable.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Pompom Crossing soft practice path, warm morning. The soft coral stop disc glows gently at
the path start. Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown pigtails) and Opa (warm green, soft bird-like
elder) stand together holding hands, watching the disc. Then the coral disc fades and the
soft green go disc lights up — a gentle colour transition. Kiko's face brightens: "Green!"
Opa smiles. Two round colour discs on the soft grass, wide stepping-stone band stretching
across. Soft pastel colours, warm light, rounded safe shapes, no other characters, {style}
{camera} {lighting}

The Pompom Crossing background is locked from the first frame; keep the stepping-stone band,
colour discs, soft grass and rounded surroundings stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

Medium shot showing both characters and the colour discs. Camera holds steady on the disc
as it transitions from coral to green. A gentle close-up on Kiko's face as she notices the
change. Then back to medium two-shot.

## Dialogue

```text
Opa: Wait for green.
Kiko: Green!
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-3 sec | Soft coral stop disc glows; Kiko and Opa watch | Medium, disc visible |
| 3-6 sec | Coral fades; soft green go disc lights up | Close-up on disc |
| 6-9 sec | Kiko brightens: "Green!" | Close-up on Kiko |
| 9-12 sec | Opa smiles: "Now we can go." | Medium two-shot |

## Sound

A soft, gentle "tick" as the colour transitions — natural, not mechanical. Kiko's "Green!"
is warm and delighted. No music, no electronic beep, no traffic signal sound.

## Emotion

Learning to read the colour signal. Kiko discovers that green means "now we can go" —
colour communicates without words. The moment is warm and celebratory in a small, natural way.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No traffic light, no red/green traffic signal, no "walk" sign, no crossing guard, no urban
infrastructure, no text on signs. The colour discs are soft, rounded, and part of the
practice path — not traffic equipment.

## Negative Prompt

low quality, blurry, deformed, extra limbs, text, watermark, photorealistic, horror, scary,
dark lighting, traffic light, red/green traffic signal, "walk" sign, crossing guard, urban
infrastructure, text on signs, road, asphalt, cars, traffic, engines, electronic beep,
mechanical sound, cinematic LUT, blue tint, green tint, orange shift, HDR look, fast
movement, sudden camera motion, static talking pose, characters frozen, background music,
music, melody, song, soundtrack, extra characters, redesigned path, missing colour discs

## QA Checklist

- [ ] Kiko + Opa identity preserved; expressions match emotional beat.
- [ ] Pompom Crossing identity preserved: stepping-stone band, colour discs, soft grass.
- [ ] No road, no asphalt, no cars, no traffic, no urban elements.
- [ ] The colour transition reads soft and natural; not like a traffic light.
- [ ] "Green!" reads as warm discovery; not excitement about crossing traffic.
- [ ] No text on the colour discs; pure colour signal.
- [ ] No on-screen text; calm but alive; no frozen pose.

#### BLD-EP15 — Shot 05 — Look Both Ways (Action)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP15 — Stop, Look, Cross |
| Shot | 05 / 08 |
| Duration | 12 seconds |
| Location | Pompom Crossing — proposed soft crossing practice path |
| Characters | Kiko, Opa |
| Time of Day | Warm Morning |
| Spine step | ACTION |

## Purpose

Teach the "look" step: Kiko and Opa slowly look right and left together. The world is calm
and clear — this is the visual confirmation that it's safe to cross.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Kiko and Opa, still holding hands, begin to turn their heads slowly to
the right. The movement is deliberate and calm — a shared ritual.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 04. The green disc is now lit; Kiko and Opa have acknowledged
"Green!" Now they look both ways before stepping onto the path. Background remains locked.

## Environment Anchors

- Same Pompom Crossing practice path; stepping-stone band and green disc visible.
- Kiko and Opa holding hands, standing at the path start.
- The world around them is calm and clear — soft grass, open space.
- No road, no asphalt, no cars, no traffic.
- No new props, no new characters, no background movement.

## Background Object Lock

Identical to Shots 01–04. Background locked from first frame. Only Kiko and Opa move
(looking right, then left). The stepping-stone band, colour discs, and soft grass remain
stable.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Pompom Crossing soft practice path, warm morning. Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown pigtails)
and Opa (warm green, soft bird-like elder) stand together holding hands at the path start.
The green go disc is lit. Together, they slowly turn their heads to the right, then to the
left — looking both ways. The world around them is calm and clear: soft green grass, open
space, warm morning light. No cars, no traffic, no danger. Kiko says: "Right... left!" with
a small smile. Soft pastel colours, warm light, rounded safe shapes, no other characters,
{style} {camera} {lighting}

The Pompom Crossing background is locked from the first frame; keep the stepping-stone band,
colour discs, soft grass and rounded surroundings stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

Medium two-shot at child eye level. Camera follows their gaze as they look right, then
left — a gentle pan movement that mirrors their head turns. Then settles back to medium
as Kiko repeats the action.

## Dialogue

```text
Opa: Look right... and left.
Kiko: Right... left!
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-3 sec | Kiko and Opa slowly look to the right | Medium, gentle pan right |
| 3-6 sec | They slowly look to the left | Medium, gentle pan left |
| 6-9 sec | Kiko repeats: "Right... left!" with a small smile | Medium hold |
| 9-12 sec | Opa smiles: "All clear." | Medium two-shot |

## Sound

A quiet moment — silence for the looking action. Kiko's "Right... left!" repetition is
playful and rhythmic, like a learning game. Soft playground ambience continues.

## Emotion

The "look" ritual becomes a game. Kiko enjoys the rhythm of looking right and left —
"Right... left!" is almost like a dance. The world is calm, the path is clear, and the
ritual feels safe and fun.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No cars passing, no traffic, no "it's clear" from a distance, no rushing, no "let's run."
The looking is slow, deliberate, and thorough — modeling careful behavior.

## Negative Prompt

low quality, blurry, deformed, extra limbs, text, watermark, photorealistic, horror, scary,
dark lighting, cars passing, traffic, "it's clear" from distance, rushing, "let's run," road,
asphalt, engines, sirens, urban street, crossing guard, traffic light, cinematic LUT, blue
tint, green tint, orange shift, HDR look, fast movement, sudden camera motion, static
talking pose, characters frozen, background music, music, melody, song, soundtrack, extra
characters, redesigned path, missing colour discs

## QA Checklist

- [ ] Kiko + Opa identity preserved; expressions match emotional beat.
- [ ] Pompom Crossing identity preserved: stepping-stone band, colour discs, soft grass.
- [ ] No road, no asphalt, no cars, no traffic, no urban elements.
- [ ] The looking action reads slow and deliberate; not rushed.
- [ ] "Right... left!" reads as playful learning; not anxious checking.
- [ ] The world is calm and clear — no danger implied.
- [ ] No on-screen text; calm but alive; no frozen pose.

#### BLD-EP15 — Shot 06 — Crossing Together (Action)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP15 — Stop, Look, Cross |
| Shot | 06 / 08 |
| Duration | 15 seconds |
| Location | Pompom Crossing — proposed soft crossing practice path |
| Characters | Kiko, Opa |
| Time of Day | Warm Morning |
| Spine step | ACTION |

## Purpose

The core crossing action: Kiko and Opa step onto the stepping-stone band together, holding
hands, and cross slowly and carefully. Each step is deliberate — this models safe crossing
behavior.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Kiko and Opa, still holding hands, take their first step onto the soft
stepping-stone band. The stone is wide, flat, and safe underfoot.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 05. They have looked both ways; now they step onto the path.
Background remains locked.

## Environment Anchors

- Same Pompom Crossing practice path; stepping-stone band stretches across soft grass.
- Two round colour discs (green lit) visible behind them.
- Kiko and Opa holding hands, stepping onto the stones.
- No road, no asphalt, no cars, no traffic.
- No new props, no new characters, no background movement.

## Background Object Lock

Identical to Shots 01–05. Background locked from first frame. Only Kiko and Opa move
across the stepping-stone band. The colour discs, soft grass, and rounded surroundings
remain stable.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Pompom Crossing soft practice path, warm morning. Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown pigtails)
and Opa (warm green, soft bird-like elder) hold hands and step onto the wide soft stepping-stone
band together. They take slow, careful steps — one stone at a time. The stones are round, flat,
and pastel-coloured, set in soft green grass. The green go disc glows behind them. Kiko counts
softly: "One step... two steps..." Both characters move with calm confidence. Soft pastel
colours, warm light, rounded safe shapes, no other characters, {style} {camera} {lighting}

The Pompom Crossing background is locked from the first frame; keep the stepping-stone band,
colour discs, soft grass and rounded surroundings stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

Medium shot at child eye level, following Kiko and Opa as they step across the stones.
Camera moves with them in a gentle lateral tracking shot — slow and steady, matching their
pace. A slight downward tilt shows their feet on the stones.

## Dialogue

```text
Kiko: One step... two steps...
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-3 sec | Kiko and Opa step onto the first stone together | Medium, gentle tracking |
| 3-7 sec | They step to the second stone; Kiko: "One step..." | Tracking continues |
| 7-11 sec | They step to the third stone: "...two steps..." | Tracking continues |
| 11-15 sec | They reach the far side; still holding hands | Wide two-shot |

## Sound

Soft stepping-stone sounds — gentle "tok tok" as feet touch the pastel stones. Kiko's
counting is playful and rhythmic. Soft playground ambience continues. No music, no rush.

## Emotion

The crossing itself — slow, careful, together. Kiko counts the steps like a game, making
the safety ritual enjoyable. Opa's steady presence provides comfort. The shared movement
reinforces trust.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No running, no jumping, no "hurry up," no skipping, no competitive crossing, no looking
back at traffic. The crossing is slow, deliberate, and cooperative — modeling safe behavior.

## Negative Prompt

low quality, blurry, deformed, extra limbs, text, watermark, photorealistic, horror, scary,
dark lighting, running, jumping, "hurry up," skipping, competitive crossing, looking back
at traffic, road, asphalt, cars, traffic, engines, sirens, urban street, crossing guard,
traffic light, cinematic LUT, blue tint, green tint, orange shift, HDR look, fast movement,
sudden camera motion, static talking pose, characters frozen, background music, music,
melody, song, soundtrack, extra characters, redesigned path, missing colour discs

## QA Checklist

- [ ] Kiko + Opa identity preserved; expressions match emotional beat.
- [ ] Pompom Crossing identity preserved: stepping-stone band, colour discs, soft grass.
- [ ] No road, no asphalt, no cars, no traffic, no urban elements.
- [ ] The crossing reads slow and careful; not rushed or playful in a dangerous way.
- [ ] Kiko's counting reads as a learning game; not anxious.
- [ ] The stepping-stone band is wide and soft; safe underfoot.
- [ ] No on-screen text; calm but alive; no frozen pose.

#### BLD-EP15 — Shot 07 — Safe Arrival (Relief)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP15 — Stop, Look, Cross |
| Shot | 07 / 08 |
| Duration | 12 seconds |
| Location | Pompom Crossing — proposed soft crossing practice path |
| Characters | Kiko, Opa |
| Time of Day | Warm Morning |
| Spine step | RELIEF |

## Purpose

The emotional payoff: Kiko and Opa have crossed safely. Kiko smiles proudly and says
"We did it safely!" — the relief and accomplishment of completing the crossing together.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Kiko and Opa reach the far side of the stepping-stone band. Kiko's
face lights up with a proud, warm smile. They are still holding hands.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 06. They have crossed the stepping-stone band; now they
arrive safely on the other side. Background remains locked.

## Environment Anchors

- Same Pompom Crossing practice path; stepping-stone band now behind them.
- Two round colour discs visible in the background.
- Kiko and Opa standing on soft grass on the far side, still holding hands.
- No road, no asphalt, no cars, no traffic.
- No new props, no new characters, no background movement.

## Background Object Lock

Identical to Shots 01–06. Background locked from first frame. Only Kiko and Opa move.
The stepping-stone band, colour discs, and soft grass remain stable.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Pompom Crossing soft practice path, warm morning. Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown pigtails)
and Opa (warm green, soft bird-like elder) reach the far side of the stepping-stone band.
They stand on soft grass, still holding hands. Kiko's face lights up with a proud, warm
smile. She says: "We did it safely!" Opa smiles warmly. The stepping-stone band stretches
behind them, colour discs visible in the background. Soft pastel colours, warm light,
rounded safe shapes, no other characters, {style} {camera} {lighting}

The Pompom Crossing background is locked from the first frame; keep the stepping-stone band,
colour discs, soft grass and rounded surroundings stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

Medium shot on Kiko as she reaches the far side; Opa beside her. Camera holds steady on
Kiko's proud face as she delivers the line. A gentle pull-back to show both characters
standing safely on the grass.

## Dialogue

```text
Kiko: We did it safely!
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-3 sec | Kiko and Opa step onto the far grass; still holding hands | Medium on Kiko |
| 3-6 sec | Kiko smiles proudly: "We did it safely!" | Medium hold |
| 6-9 sec | Opa smiles: "Yes, we did." | Medium two-shot |
| 9-12 sec | Both stand together, warm and proud | Gentle pull-back |

## Sound

Kiko's voice is warm and proud — "We did it safely!" is a quiet celebration. Opa's
"Yes, we did" is warm and affirming. Soft playground ambience continues. No music, no
triumphant fanfare.

## Emotion

Relief and accomplishment. Kiko and Opa crossed safely by following the steps: stop, look,
hold hands. The feeling is gentle pride — not boastful, just happy and safe.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No celebration, no cheering, no "we beat the cars" (no cars exist), no dramatic relief,
no high five, no victory dance. The accomplishment is quiet and warm — a shared moment
of safety.

## Negative Prompt

low quality, blurry, deformed, extra limbs, text, watermark, photorealistic, horror, scary,
dark lighting, celebration, cheering, "we beat the cars," dramatic relief, high five,
victory dance, road, asphalt, cars, traffic, engines, sirens, urban street, crossing guard,
traffic light, cinematic LUT, blue tint, green tint, orange shift, HDR look, fast movement,
sudden camera motion, static talking pose, characters frozen, background music, music,
melody, song, soundtrack, extra characters, redesigned path, missing colour discs

## QA Checklist

- [ ] Kiko + Opa identity preserved; expressions match emotional beat.
- [ ] Pompom Crossing identity preserved: stepping-stone band, colour discs, soft grass.
- [ ] No road, no asphalt, no cars, no traffic, no urban elements.
- [ ] "We did it safely!" reads as proud accomplishment; not boastful.
- [ ] The relief is warm and gentle; no dramatic celebration.
- [ ] Both characters remain holding hands — continuity from Shot 06.
- [ ] No on-screen text; calm but alive; no frozen pose.

#### BLD-EP15 — Shot 08 — Warm Closing (Lesson)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP15 — Stop, Look, Cross |
| Shot | 08 / 08 |
| Duration | 12 seconds |
| Location | Pompom Crossing — proposed soft crossing practice path |
| Characters | Kiko, Opa |
| Time of Day | Warm Morning |
| Spine step | LESSON |

## Purpose

The warm closing shot: Kiko and Opa stand together on the far side of the crossing path.
They deliver the repeated phrase "Stop, look, hold a hand" one final time, sealing the lesson
with a friendly goodbye.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Kiko and Opa stand together on soft grass, the stepping-stone band
behind them. Both face the camera with warm, relaxed smiles. They are still holding hands.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 07. They have crossed safely; now they deliver the final
lesson together. Background remains locked.

## Environment Anchors

- Same Pompom Crossing practice path; stepping-stone band and colour discs behind them.
- Kiko and Opa standing on soft grass, holding hands, facing camera.
- No road, no asphalt, no cars, no traffic.
- No new props, no new characters, no background movement.

## Background Object Lock

Identical to Shots 01–07. Background locked from first frame. Only Kiko and Opa move
(wave). The stepping-stone band, colour discs, and soft grass remain stable.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Pompom Crossing soft practice path, warm morning. Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown pigtails)
and Opa (warm green, soft bird-like elder) stand together on soft grass, holding hands, facing
the camera. The stepping-stone band and colour discs are visible behind them. Both have warm,
relaxed smiles. They say together: "Stop, look, hold a hand." Then they give a small gentle
wave. Soft pastel colours, warm light, rounded safe shapes, no other characters, {style}
{camera} {lighting}

The Pompom Crossing background is locked from the first frame; keep the stepping-stone band,
colour discs, soft grass and rounded surroundings stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

Medium shot at child eye level, both characters centered in frame. Camera holds steady for
the final moment. A very gentle, almost imperceptible pull-back to show the full warm scene.
The shot fades to soft warmth at the end.

## Dialogue

```text
Kiko & Opa: Stop, look, hold a hand.
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-3 sec | Kiko and Opa stand together, facing camera, warm smiles | Medium hold |
| 3-6 sec | Both say: "Stop, look, hold a hand." | Medium hold |
| 6-9 sec | They give a small gentle wave to the camera | Medium hold |
| 9-12 sec | Warm smiles; the scene holds for a soft, gentle fade | Gentle pull-back |

## Sound

Soft playground ambience: birds, light breeze. Both voices together on the repeated phrase —
warm, sincere, and friendly. No music, no outro sting. Natural ambience carries to the end.

## Emotion

Warm closure. The shared crossing, the shared words, the shared wave — everything reinforces
that safety is a learned ritual, not a rule. The lesson is complete, and the feeling is one
of gentle accomplishment.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No moralizing, no lecture, no adult voice-over, no on-screen text, no dramatic music, no
lesson-on-screen, no exaggerated wave, no preachy tone. The repeated phrase is delivered as
a shared discovery, not a rule being taught. The wave is friendly and inclusive — inviting
the viewer into the moment.

## Negative Prompt

low quality, blurry, deformed, extra limbs, text, watermark, photorealistic, horror, scary,
dark lighting, moralizing, lecture, adult voice-over, on-screen text, dramatic music,
lesson-on-screen, exaggerated wave, preachy tone, road, asphalt, cars, traffic, engines,
sirens, urban street, crossing guard, traffic light, cinematic LUT, blue tint, green tint,
orange shift, HDR look, fast movement, sudden camera motion, static talking pose, characters
frozen, background music, music, melody, song, soundtrack, extra characters, redesigned
path, missing colour discs

## QA Checklist

- [ ] Kiko + Opa identity preserved; final expressions warm and relaxed.
- [ ] Pompom Crossing identity preserved: stepping-stone band, colour discs, soft grass.
- [ ] No road, no asphalt, no cars, no traffic, no urban elements.
- [ ] "Stop, look, hold a hand" delivered as shared discovery, not lecture.
- [ ] The wave is gentle and friendly; not exaggerated.
- [ ] No on-screen text; calm but alive; no frozen pose.
- [ ] The closing feels warm and complete — no loose ends.

## BLD-EP16 — "Careful, It's Hot!" (viewing #16)

- **Tema:** Sıcak şeylere dokunmamak · **Mekan:** Kiko's Home — Kitchen Nook · **Kadro:** Kiko, Opa (veya Mimi)
- **Repeated phrase:** "Hot! We don't touch."
- **Spine:** (1) Masada sıcak bir çorba/çay kupası (hafif buhar). (2) Kiko merakla uzanır. (3) Opa nazikçe
  "Careful — it's hot." (4) Kiko elini geri çeker; birlikte soğumasını beklerler / üfleyip soğuturlar. (5) Güvenle,
  ılık olunca dokunur. (6) "Hot! We don't touch." (7) Öğrendiği için gururlu. (8) Sıcak kapanış.
- **Safe-exposure:** Gerçek yanık/ateş/ocak alevi YOK. Sadece hafif buhar wisp'i + "bekle/soğut" mesajı.

### Scene Definition Starter

- **Kapsam kararı:** Tek ana set olarak **Kiko's Home — Kitchen Nook / low round table** kullanılır.
  Ev tek bağlantılı living space olarak korunur; mutfak ayrı oda gibi yeniden tasarlanmaz.
- **Kadro kararı:** **Kiko + Opa**. Opa sakin yetişkin helper olarak sıcak nesneye dokunmama davranışını modeller.
- **Prop:** Bir yuvarlak kase veya yumuşak kulplu cup içinde **warm soup**. Yalnızca 1-2 çok hafif buhar çizgisi;
  ocak, ateş, kettle, fırın, kaynar dökülme yok.
- **Safe-exposure:** Yanık, acı, tehlike gösterilmez. Kiko'nun eli nesneye değmeden durur ve geri çekilir.

| Shot | Spine | Scene amacı | Kısa tanım |
|---:|---|---|---|
| 01 | Problem | Sıcak kaseyi fark etme | Kiko low round table üstündeki buharlı kaseyi görür. |
| 02 | Feeling | Merakla uzanma | Kiko yavaşça elini uzatır ama henüz dokunmaz. |
| 03 | Support | Opa uyarır | Opa nazikçe: "Careful — it's hot." |
| 04 | Action | Eli geri çekme | Kiko elini göğsüne çeker: "Hot." |
| 05 | Action | Bekleme | Opa ve Kiko ellerini dizlerinde tutarak kaseden uzak bekler. |
| 06 | Relief | Ilıdı | Buhar azalır; Opa kaşıkla hafifçe karıştırır, Kiko izler. |
| 07 | Relief | Güvenli deneme | Opa onayladıktan sonra Kiko ılık çorbayı güvenle koklar/tadar. |
| 08 | Lesson | Sıcak kapanış | "Hot! We don't touch." sıcak bir gülümsemeyle kapanır. |

#### BLD-EP16 — Shot 01 — Warm Soup on the Table (Problem)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP16 — Careful, It's Hot! |
| Shot | 01 / 08 |
| Duration | 15 seconds |
| Location | Kiko's Home — Kitchen Nook / low round table |
| Characters | Kiko, Opa |
| Time of Day | Warm Daytime |
| Spine step | PROBLEM |

## Purpose

Open with a simple, readable curiosity moment: Kiko notices a rounded soup bowl on the low round table
with faint friendly steam rising from it. Opa is nearby, calm and warm. The scene opens with care
and curiosity — the soup is inviting but not yet safe to touch.

## Opening Hook

First 3–5 seconds: Kiko approaches the low round table and notices the rounded soup bowl with very
faint steam wisps rising from it. The object is instantly readable, soft, and safe-looking — warm,
not dangerous. Opa is nearby, calm and present.

## Continuity

First story shot, after the shared Brave Little Days opening bumper. This shot establishes the
Kitchen Nook world identity and the warm soup scenario. The first-frame still = **Episode Colour
Master**. Maintain Kiko + Opa identity, Kiko's Home warm kitchen nook identity, warm daytime light.
Do not redesign the kitchen nook.

## Environment Anchors

- Kiko's Home — Kitchen Nook: a cozy, rounded kitchen nook with warm daytime light.
- One low round table in soft pastel tones; the rounded soup bowl/cup sits on it.
- Faint friendly steam wisps rise from the bowl — 1–2 very soft lines only.
- Opa stands nearby, calm and present.
- No stove, no kettle, no fire, no boiling water visible. No other characters, no background movement.

## Background Object Lock

Background locked from first frame. The Kitchen Nook — low round table, warm walls, rounded furniture,
soft light — remains stable. Only Kiko, Opa, the soup bowl, and the faint steam wisps move.
No characters appear or disappear.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Kiko's Home Kitchen Nook, warm daytime. A low round table holds a single rounded soup bowl with very
faint friendly steam wisps rising — 1–2 soft lines only, no heavy steam. Kiko (coral pink shirt,
brown pigtails) approaches the table with a bright curious smile, noticing the warm soup. Opa (warm
green, soft bird-like elder) stands nearby, calm and present. Soft pastel colours, warm light, rounded
safe kitchen shapes, no stove, no kettle, no fire, no other characters, {style} {camera} {lighting}

The Kiko's Home Kitchen Nook background is locked from the first frame; keep the low round table,
rounded furniture and warm daytime light stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

32mm wide at child eye level establishing the Kitchen Nook and low round table; slow settle to medium
on Kiko, Opa, and the steaming soup bowl. Stable settle only. No fast zooms, no dramatic angles.

## Dialogue

```text
Kiko: What's that?

Opa: Warm soup.
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-4 sec | Kitchen Nook visible; low round table with steaming soup bowl | Wide |
| 4-8 sec | Kiko approaches and notices the steam: "What's that?" | Settle to medium |
| 8-12 sec | Opa smiles warmly: "Warm soup." | Medium two-shot |
| 12-15 sec | Kiko looks at the bowl with bright curiosity | Medium hold |

## Sound

#### BLD-EP16 — Shot 05 — Waiting (Action)

smell and taste. The camera catches her delighted expression. Steady, warm movement. No fast cuts,
no dramatic angles.

## Dialogue

```text
Opa: Now it's safe.

Kiko: Mmm, warm!
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-3 sec | Opa looks at the bowl, then at Kiko: "Now it's safe." | Medium on Opa |
| 3-6 sec | Kiko leans in carefully to smell the warm soup | Slow push-in on Kiko |
| 6-9 sec | Small, gentle taste — face lights up with delight | Close-up hold |
| 9-12 sec | "Mmm, warm!" — happy and proud | Medium two-shot |

## Sound

Kiko's "Mmm" is warm and natural — the pleasure of tasting something good. "Warm!" is delighted
but calm. Opa's voice is reassuring. Soft home ambience continues. No music, no triumphant fanfare,
no dramatic sting.

## Emotion

Reward and discovery. After patience and waiting, Kiko gets to experience the warm soup — and it's
wonderful. The lesson is complete: hot things become warm, and warm things are safe and pleasant.
Kiko's pride comes not from being praised, but from having waited and been rewarded.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

No burning, no "ouch," no steam burn, no "too hot" face, no spilling, no mess, no dramatic
tasting. The soup is genuinely warm and safe — Kiko's experience confirms it. The tasting is
gentle and natural.

## BLD-EP17 — "My First Day" ⭐🆕 (viewing #17)

- **Tema:** İlk Learning Room günü (ayrılık kaygısı) · **Mekan:** 🆕 **Learning Room** (warm preschool learning cottage) · **Kadro:** Kiko, Opa (bırakan), Amara (yeni arkadaş)
- **Repeated phrase:** "I'll be back soon."
- **Spine:** (1) Kiko ilk Learning Room gününe gelir, Opa'nın yanında durur. (2) Ayrılığa üzülür/tedirgin. (3) Opa "I'll be back
  soon." + güven verir. (4) Kiko içeri girer, ilgi çeken bir şey bulur (boya/kitap). (5) Amara ile tanışır, oynarlar.
  (6) Gün eğlenceli geçer. (7) Opa döner — sevinç. (8) "I'll be back soon" gerçek oldu; Learning Room güvenli.
- **🆕 Yeni canon / hassas:** Learning Room gerçek okul sınıfı gibi değil, mevcut canonundaki sıcak öğrenme kulübesi
  gibi kalır. "İlk gün / drop-off" davranışı üretimden önce onaylanmalıdır. Ayrılık kaygısı çok nazik;
  ağlama krizi YOK, kısa bir hüzün → hızlı güven.

### Scene Definition Starter — Pending Learning Room Production Approval

- **Kapsam kararı:** Tek ana set olarak **Learning Room — Entrance / Activity Area** kullanılır. Burası gerçek
  okul sınıfı değil; canon tanımına uygun **warm preschool learning cottage** olarak kalır.
- **Kadro kararı:** **Kiko, Opa, Amara**. Amara yeni canon değil, mevcut karakterdir; "ilk arkadaş" desteği verir.
- **Production notu:** Learning Room bible içinde status "Design" ve hero view durumu belirsiz/eksik göründüğü için
  üretimden önce Learning Room görsel referansı kilitlenmelidir. Canon dosyası bu draftta değiştirilmez.
- **Safe-exposure:** Ayrılık kaygısı kısa ve naziktir. Opa ayrılırken Kiko terk edilmiş gibi gösterilmez; Opa
  "I'll be back soon" der, sonra gerçekten döner.

| Shot | Spine | Scene amacı | Kısa tanım |
|---:|---|---|---|
| 01 | Problem | İlk giriş | Kiko ve Opa Learning Room kapısında durur; Amara içeride masada yumuşakça el sallar. |
| 02 | Feeling | Kısa tedirginlik | Kiko Opa'nın kanat ucunu tutar: "Stay?" |
| 03 | Support | Güven sözü | Opa diz hizasına iner: "I'll be back soon." |
| 04 | Action | İçeri küçük adım | Kiko aktivite masasına doğru bir adım atar; Amara yer açar. |
| 05 | Action | İlk oyun | Amara büyük yuvarlak crayonları gösterir; Kiko bir renk seçer. |
| 06 | Relief | Arkadaşlık başlar | Kiko ve Amara aynı kağıda iki basit şekil çizer. |
| 07 | Relief | Opa döner | Opa kapıda yeniden görünür; Kiko sevinçle bakar. |
| 08 | Lesson | Sıcak kapanış | Opa: "I came back." Kiko: "I'll be back soon." |

#### BLD-EP17 — Shot 01 — At the Learning Room Door (Problem)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP17 — My First Day |

Open the episode at the Learning Room doorway: Kiko and Opa arrive at the warm learning cottage.

The space reads as a cozy learning cottage, not a school classroom.

## Opening Hook

First 3–5 seconds: Kiko and Opa stand at the Learning Room doorway. The warm cottage interior is
visible — a large round wooden table (LR-TABLE-01) and a soft chalkboard (LR-BOARD-01) on the
far wall. Amara, already seated at the table, gives a gentle, friendly wave.

## Continuity

First story shot, after the shared Brave Little Days opening bumper. This shot establishes the
Learning Room world identity and the drop-off scenario. The first-frame still = **Episode Colour
Master**. Maintain Kiko + Opa + Amara identity, Learning Room warm cottage identity, warm
morning light. Do not redesign the Learning Room.

## Environment Anchors

- Learning Room — Entrance / Activity Area: warm preschool learning cottage, NOT a school classroom.
- `LR-TABLE-01` visible inside: a large round wooden activity table with soft edges.
- `LR-BOARD-01` softly visible on the far wall: a soft chalkboard with rounded frame.
- No desks in rows, no fluorescent light, no modern screens, no clocks, no school bells.
- Warm morning light through a small round window; soft wooden floor, rounded furniture.
- Amara seated at the table, visible through the open doorway.

## Background Object Lock

Background locked from first frame. The Learning Room interior — LR-TABLE-01, LR-BOARD-01,
wooden floor, warm walls, rounded furniture — remains stable. Only Kiko, Opa, and Amara move.
No characters appear or disappear.

## Visual Prompt


| 12-15 sec | Opa smiles warmly: "I'll be back soon." | Medium two-shot |

## Sound

Soft warm ambience: birds outside, gentle breeze through the round window, very faint sound of
Amara shifting in her chair. Kiko's voice is soft and questioning — not scared, just seeking
reassurance. Opa's voice is warm and steady. No music, no dramatic sting.

## Emotion

First-day arrival: curiosity mixed with mild hesitation. Kiko sees a new place and a familiar
face (Amara) inside, but still wants Opa nearby. The feeling is natural and age-appropriate —
not fear, not separation anxiety crisis, just a small "will you stay?" moment.

No crying, no clinging, no "don't leave me" desperation, no screaming, no panic, no locked
door, no pushing away. The separation anxiety is very gentle — a brief hesitation, not a

#### BLD-EP17 — Shot 04 — A Small Step In (Action)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP17 — My First Day |
| Shot | 04 / 08 |

staying.

## Opening Hook

First 2–3 seconds: Kiko glances back at Opa at the doorway, then turns toward the interior.
The glance is brief — a natural "are you still there?" check before stepping forward.

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 03. Opa has just delivered "I'll be back soon." Kiko's face has
softened. Now she acts on the trust — a small step inside. Background remains locked.

## Environment Anchors

- Same Learning Room doorway and interior; LR-TABLE-01 and LR-BOARD-01 visible.
- Amara at the table, making space with a welcoming gesture.
- Kiko crosses the doorway threshold — moving from outside to inside.
- Opa remains visible at the doorway behind Kiko.
- No new props, no new characters, no background movement.

## Background Object Lock

Identical to Shots 01–03. Background locked from first frame. Only Kiko, Opa, and Amara move.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Learning Room warm preschool learning cottage, warm morning. Kiko (coral pink shirt, brown
pigtails) glances back at Opa (warm green, soft bird-like elder) at the doorway one last time,
then turns and takes a small, careful step into the room. Her expression is quiet and
determined — not afraid, just thoughtful. Amara (yellow shirt, purple short overalls, yellow
bow headband, two dark brown puff buns) sits at the large round wooden table (LR-TABLE-01) and
shifts slightly to make space, smiling welcomingly. LR-BOARD-01 softly visible on the far wall.
```

#### BLD-EP17 — Shot 06 — Friendship Begins (Relief)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP17 — My First Day |
| Shot | 06 / 08 |
| Duration | 15 seconds |
| Location | Learning Room — Entrance / Activity Area |

| Time of Day | Warm Morning |
| Spine step | RELIEF |

## Purpose

The friendship payoff: Kiko and Amara draw together on the same piece of paper — Kiko draws a

fully dissolved into playful connection.

## Opening Hook

## Continuity

Direct continuation from Shot 05. The crayons are on the table; Kiko and Amara are engaged.
Now they begin drawing together — the natural next step from exploring crayons to using them.
Background remains locked.

## Environment Anchors

- Same Learning Room interior; LR-TABLE-01 is the drawing surface.
- LR-BOARD-01 softly visible on the far wall.
- One sheet of soft paper on the table; two large crayons in use (coral, yellow).
- Kiko and Amara standing/seated at the table, focused on the paper.
- No other characters, no background movement.

## Background Object Lock

Identical to Shots 01–05. Background locked from first frame. Only Kiko, Amara, and the
crayons move. The Learning Room interior, LR-TABLE-01, LR-BOARD-01, and paper remain stable.


## Emotion

Friendship through shared creation. Drawing together on the same paper is a cooperative act —
neither child dominates, both contribute. The circle and square are simple, but the act of

engaged.

## Safe-Exposure Notes

## BLD-EP18 — "Hello, New Friend" (viewing #18)

- **Tema:** Yeni arkadaş edinmek · **Mekan:** Central Square / Friendship Meadow · **Kadro:** Kiko, yeni bir çocuk (ör. Sofia/Luca)
- **Repeated phrase:** "Can I play too?"
- **Spine:** (1) Kiko tek başına oynayan bir çocuğu görür. (2) Utangaç, tereddüt eder. (3) Cesaret toplar
  (Mimi destek). (4) "Hi, I'm Kiko. Can I play too?" (5) Yeni arkadaş sevinir. (6) Birlikte oynarlar. (7) Yeni dostluk.
  (8) "Can I play too?" — arkadaşlık kurmak.
- **Not:** Yeni canon yok (mevcut kadrodan bir çocuk).

### Scene Definition Starter

- **Kapsam kararı:** Tek ana set olarak **Friendship Meadow — Rest Circle / Group Game Space edge** kullanılır.
  Arkadaşlık temasını doğal olarak destekler; büyük kalabalık yok.
- **Kadro kararı:** **Kiko, Mimi, Sofia**. Sofia mevcut karakterdir ve yaratıcı/renkli oyun üzerinden yeni
  arkadaşlık kurmak için uygundur.
- **Prop:** Bir küçük yuvarlak oyun örtüsü + büyük güvenli renk kartları / yumuşak bloklar. Art supplies varsa
  büyük, yuvarlak, keskin uçsuz olmalıdır.
- **Safe-exposure:** Sofia "dışlayan" değildir; tek başına sakin oynuyordur. Kiko'nun çekingenliği kısa ve
  yumuşaktır, sosyal reddedilme yok.

#### BLD-EP18 — Shot 01 — A New Friend Nearby (Problem)

## Scene Context

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Episode | Brave Little Days EP18 — Hello, New Friend |
| Shot | 01 / 08 |
| Duration | 15 seconds |
| Location | Friendship Meadow — Rest Circle / Group Game Space edge |
| Characters | Kiko, Mimi, Sofia |
| Time of Day | Warm Daytime |
| Spine step | PROBLEM |

## Purpose

Open with a readable discovery: Sofia sits alone on a small round play blanket arranging
large soft colour cards. Kiko and Mimi notice her from a short distance — the "new friend"
moment begins with curiosity, not conflict.

## Opening Hook

First 3–5 seconds: Sofia sits cross-legged on the small round play blanket, carefully
placing 4–5 large soft colour cards in a gentle pattern. She is calm and absorbed in her
play. Kiko and Mimi stand a few steps away, noticing her for the first time.

## Continuity

First story shot after the shared Brave Little Days opening bumper. This shot establishes
the Friendship Meadow setting, the three characters, and the colour-card play activity.
Background: soft green meadow, low rest-circle seating, warm daytime light.

## Environment Anchors

- Friendship Meadow — Rest Circle / Group Game Space edge; soft grass, low rounded seating.
- One small round play blanket on the grass.
- 4–5 large soft colour cards / blocks arranged by Sofia on the blanket.
- Sofia seated on the blanket; Kiko and Mimi standing a short distance away.
- No other characters, no background movement, no hard surfaces.

## Background Object Lock

Background locked from first frame. Friendship Meadow meadow, rest-circle seating, and
warm daytime light remain stable. Only Kiko, Mimi, Sofia, and the colour cards move.

## Visual Prompt

```text
Friendship Meadow — Rest Circle / Group Game Space edge, warm daytime. Sofia (wavy dark
brown hair with pink flower clip, denim blue overalls with pink flower patch, white shirt
with colorful trim) sits cross-legged on a small round play blanket on soft green grass,

pink shirt, brown pigtails) and Mimi (soft blue rabbit, yellow t-shirt, long floppy ears)
stand a few steps away, watching Sofia with quiet curiosity. Soft pastel colours, warm
daytime light, rounded safe meadow shapes, no other characters, {style} {camera} {lighting}

The Friendship Meadow background is locked from the first frame; keep the soft grass,
rest-circle seating and rounded meadow shapes stable.

Do not display dialogue as on-screen text. No speech bubbles. No captions. No text.
```

## Camera Direction

32mm wide at child eye level establishing the Rest Circle area and the three characters;
slow settle to medium on Kiko, Mimi, and Sofia with the colour cards visible. Stable
settle only.

## Dialogue

```text
Kiko: She is playing.
Mimi: Let's say hi.
```

## Shot Breakdown

| Time | Action | Camera |
|---|---|---|
| 0-4 sec | Friendship Meadow visible; Sofia arranges colour cards on the blanket | Wide |
| 4-8 sec | Kiko notices Sofia: "She is playing." | Settle |

#### BLD-EP18 — Shot 04 — Hi, I'm Kiko (Action)
